ityadhyetavyatvavidhānādeva pravṛttiḥ setsyati iti cet maivamtathā vidhānepi tadīyavedāṅgatvapratipādakaprayojanānabhidhāne teṣāṃ pravṛtteranupapatteḥtathā hi purā kila vedamadhītyādhyetārastvaritā bhaveyuḥdharmāddhīyeranata eva yājñikāḥ paṭhanti āhitāgnirapaśabdaṃ prayujya prāyaścittīyāṃ sārasvatīmiṣṭiṃ nirvapeditiatastadīyavedāṅgatva pratipādakaprayojanānvākhyānārthamatha śabdānuśāsanamityeva tadupāyābhāvātatha pratipadapāṭha evābhyupāya iti manyethāstarhi sa hyanabhyupāyaḥ śabdānāṃ pratipattau pratipādapāṭho bhavetśabdāpaśabda bhedenānantyācchabdānāmevaṃ hi samāmnāyate  bṛhaspatirindrāya prayojanaṃ na sidhyediti cet  maivam śabdapratipatteḥ pratipadapāṭhasādhyatvānaṅgīkārātprakṛtyādivibhāga kalpanāvatsu lakṣyeṣu sāmānyaviśeṣarūpāṇāṃ lakṣaṇānāṃ parjanyavatsakṛdeva pravṛttau bahūnāṃ martyāṃ āviveśamahāndevaḥ śabdo martyā maraṇadharmāṇo manuṣyāstānāviveśetimahatā devena pareṇa brahmaṇā sāmyamuktaṃ syātmahābhāṣyam pṛ itijagannidānaṃ sphoṭākhyo niravayavo nityaḥ śabdo brahmaiveti hariṇābhāṇi brahmakāṇḍe  anādinidhanaṃ brahma śabdatattvaṃ tadakṣaramvivartaterthabhāvena prakriyā jagato yataḥvākyapa  itinanu nāmākhyātabhedena padadvaividhyapratīteḥ kathaṃ cāturvidhyamuktamiti cet maivamprakārāntarasya prasiddhatvāttaduktaṃ prakīrṇake  dvidhā kaiścitpadaṃ bhinnaṃ caturdhā pañcadhāpi vāapoddhṛtyaiva vākyebhyaḥ prakṛtipratyayādivatkarmapravacanīyena vai pañcamena saha padasya pañcavidhatvamiti helārājo vyākhyātavānkarmapravacanīyāstu kriyāviśeṣopajanitasaṃbandhāvacchedahetava iti saṃbandhaviśeṣadyotanadvāreṇa kriyāviśeṣadyotanādupasargeṣvevantarbhavantītyabhisandhāya padacāturvidhyaṃ bhāṣyakāreṇoktaṃ yuktamiti vivektavyamnanu bhavatā sphoṭātmā nityaḥ śabda iti nijāgadyatetanna mṛṣyāmahetatra pramāṇābhāvāditi kecitatrocyate pratyakṣamevātra pramāṇamgaurītyekaṃ padamiti nānāvarṇātiriktaikapadāvagateḥ sarvajanīnatvātna hyasati bādhake padānubhavaḥ śakyo mithyeti vaktumpadārthapratītyanyathā nupapattyāpi sphoṭobhyupagantavyaḥna ca varṇebhya eva tatpratyayaḥ prādurbhavatīti parīkṣākṣamamvikalpāsahatvātkiṃ varṇāḥ samastā vyastā vārthapratyayaṃ janayanti nādyaḥ varṇānāṃ kṣaṇikānāṃ samūhāsaṃbhavātnāntyaḥ vyastavarṇebhyorthapratyayāsaṃbhavātna ca vyāsasamāsābhyāmanyaḥ prakāraḥ samastītitasmādvarṇānāṃ vācakatvānupapattau yadbalādarthapratipattiḥ sa sphoṭaḥvarṇātirikto varṇābhivyaṅgyorthapratyāyako nityaḥ śabdaḥ sphoṭa iti tadvido vadantiata eva sphuṭyate vyajyate varṇairiti sphoṭo varṇābhivyaṅgayaḥ sphuṭati sphuṭībhavatyasmādartha iti sphoṭorthapratyāyaka iti sphoṭaśabdārthamubhayathā nirāhuḥtathā coktaṃ bhagavatā patañjalinā mahābhāṣye atha gaurityatra kaḥ śabdaḥ yenoccāritena sāsnālāṅgūlakakudakhuraviṣāṇināṃ saṃpratyayo bhavati sa śabdaḥ mahābhā pṛ  itivivṛtaṃ ca kaiyaṭena vaiyākaraṇā varṇavyatiriktasya padasya vācakatvamicchantivarṇānāṃ vācakatve dvitīyādivarṇoṃccāraṇānarthakyaprasaṅgādityādinā tadvyatiriktaḥ sphoṭo nādābhivyaṅgyo vācako vistareṇa vākyapadīye vyavasthāpitaḥityantena prabandhenananu sphoṭasyāpyarthapratyāyakatvaṃ na ghaṭatevikalpāsahatvātkimabhivyaktaḥ sphoṭorthaṃ pratyāyayatyanabhivyakto vā na caramaḥ sarvādārthapratyayalakṣaṇakāryoṃtpādaprasaṅgātsphoṭasya nityatvābhyupagamena nirapekṣasya hetoḥ sadā sattvena kāryasya vilambāyogātathaitaddoṣaparijihīrṣayābhivyaktaḥ sphoṭorthaṃ pratyāyayatīti kakṣīkriyate tathāpyabhivyañjayanto varṇāḥ kiṃ pratyekamabhivyañjayanti saṃbhūya vā pakṣadvayepi varṇānāṃ vācakatvapakṣe bhavatā ye doṣā bhāṣitāsta eva sphoṭābhivyañjakatvapakṣe vyāvartanīyāḥtaduktaṃ bhaṭṭācāryermīmāṃsāślokavārtike  yasyānavayavaḥ sphoṭo vyajyate varṇabuddhibhiḥsopi paryaṃnuyogena naikenāpi vimucyatevibhaktyanteṣveva varṇeṣu suptiṅntaṃ padam pāsū iti pāṇininā te vibhaktyantāḥ padam nyāsū iti gautamena ca padasaṃjñāyā vihitatvātsaṃke tagraheṇānugrahavaśādvarṇeṣveva padabuddhirbhaviṣyatitarhi sara ityetasminpade yāvanto varṇāstāvanta eva rasa ityatrāpievaṃ vanaṃ navaṃ nadī dīnā rāmo māro rājā jārā ityādiṣvarthabhedapratītirna syāditi cennakramabhedena bhedasaṃbhavāttaduktaṃ tautātitaiḥ  yāvanto yādṛśā ye ca yadarthapratipattayevarṇāḥ prajñātasāmarthyāste tathaivāvabodhakāḥtasmādyaścobhayoḥ samo doṣo na tenaikaścodyo bhavatīti nyāyādvarṇānāmeva vācakatvopapattau nātiriktasphoṭakalpanāvakalpata iti cet tadetatkāśakuśāvalambanakalpanam vikalpānupapatteḥkiṃ varṇamātraṃ padapratyayāvalambanaṃ varṇasamūho vā nādyaḥparasparavilakṣaṇavarṇamālāyāmabhinnaṃ nimittaṃ puṣpeṣu vinā sūtraṃ mālāpratyayavadityekaṃ padamiti pratipatteranupapatteḥnāpi dvitīyaḥuccaritapradhvastānāṃ varṇānāṃ samūhabhāvāsaṃbhavāttatra hi samūhavyapadeśo ye padārthā ekasminpradeśe sahāvasthitatayā bahavonubhūyante yathaikasminpradeśe sahāvasthitatayānubhūyamāneṣu dhavakhadirapalāśādiṣu samūhavyapadeśo yathā vā gajanaraturagādiṣuna ca te varṇāstathānubhūyante utpannapradhvastatvātabhivyaktipakṣepi krameṇaivābhivyaktiḥ samūhāsaṃbhavātnāpi varṇeṣu kālpanikaḥ samūhaḥ kalpanīyaḥparasparāśrayaprasaṅgāekārthapratyāyakatvasiddhau tadupādhinā varṇeṣu padatvapratītistatsiddhāvekārthapratyāyakatvasiddhirititasmādvarṇānāṃ vācakatvāsaṃbhavātsphoṭo bhyupagantavyaḥnanu sphoṭavyañjakatāpakṣepi prāguktavikalpaprasareṇa ghaṭṭakuṭīprabhātāyitamiti cet tadetanmanorājyavijṛmbhaṇamvaiṣamyasabhavāttathā hi abhivyañjakopi prathamo dhvaniḥ sphoṭamasphuṭamabhivyanaktiuttarottarābhivyañjakakrameṇa sphuṭaṃ sphuṭataraṃ sphuṭatamamyathā svādhyāyaḥ sakṛtpaṭhayamāno nāvadhāryateabhyāsena tu sphuṭāvasāyaḥyathā vā rajatatvaṃ prathamapratītau sphuṭaṃ na cakāsticarame cetasi yathāvadabhivyajyatenādairāhitabījāyāmantyena dhvaninā sahaāvṛttiparipākāyāṃ buddhau śabdovadhāryatevākyapa  iti prāmāṇikokteḥtasmādasmācchabdādarthaṃ pratipadyāmaha iti vyavahāravaśādvarṇānāmartha vācakatvānupapatteḥprathame kāṇḍe tatrabhavadbhirbhatṛharibhirabhihitatvānniravayavamarthapratyāyakaṃ śabdatattvaṃ sphoṭākhyamabhyupagantavyamitietatsarvaṃ paramārthasaṃvillakṣaṇasattājātireva sarveṣāṃ śabdānāmartha iti mahaccāturyamāyuṣmataḥtaduktam  paryāyāṇāṃ prayogo hi yaugapadyena neṣyateparyāyeṇaiva te yasmādvadantyarthaṃ na saṃhatāḥtasmādayaṃ pakṣo na kṣodakṣama iti cet  tadetad gaganaromanthakalpamnīlalohitapītādyuparañjaka dravyabhedena sphaṭikamaṇeriva saṃbandhibhedātsattāyāstadātmanā bhedena pratipattisiddhau gosattādirūpa gotvādibhedanibandhanavyavahāravailakṣaṇyopapatteḥtathā cāptavākyam sphaṭikaṃ vimalaṃ dravyaṃ yathā yuktaṃ pṛthakapṛthaknīlalohitapītādyaistadvarṇamupalabhyatetathā hariṇāpyuktam  saṃbandhibhedātsattaiva bhidyamānā gavādiṣujātirityucyate tasyāṃ sarve śabdā vyavasthitāḥtāṃ prātipadikārthaṃ ca dhātvarthaṃ ca pracakṣatesā nityā sā mahānātmā tāmāhustvatalādayaḥāśrayabhūtaiḥ saṃbandhibhirbhidyamānā kalpitabhedā gavāśvādiṣu sattaiva mahāsāmānyameva jātiḥgotvādikamaparaṃ sāmānyaṃ paramārthatastato bhinnaṃ na bhavatigosattaiva gotvaṃ nāparamanvayi bhavatyevatasya bhāvastvatalau pā sū iti bhāvārthe tvatalādīnāṃ vidhānātsattāvācitvaṃ yuktamsā ca sattodayavyayavaidhuryānnityāsarvasya prapañcasya tadvivartatayā deśataḥ kālato vastutaśca paricchedarāhityātsā sattā mahānātmeti vyapadiśyata iti kārikādvayārthaḥdravyapadārthavādinopi naye saṃvillakṣaṇaṃ tattvameva sarvaśabdārtha iti sambandhasamuddeśe samarthitam  satyaṃ vastu ityetadvārtikavyākhyānāvasare dravyaṃ hi nityamityanena granthenāsatyopādhyavacchinaṃ brahmatattvaṃ dravyaśabdavācyaṃ sarvaśabdārtha iti nirūpitamjātiśabdārthavācino vājapyāyanasya mate gavādayaḥ ṣoḍaśako vikāra eva na prakṛtirityarthaḥyadyapi pṛthivyādayo goghaṭādīnāṃ prakṛtistathāpi na te pṛthivyādibhyastattvāntaramiti na prakṛtiḥtattvāntaropādānatvaṃ ceha prakṛtitvamabhimatamgoghaṭādīnāṃ mohātmakatā tattama iti triguṇātmakakāraṇasiddhiḥtathā hipratyekaṃ bhāvāstraiguṇyavantonubhūyanteyathā maitradāreṣu satyavatyāṃ maitrasya sukhamāvirastitaṃ prati sattvaguṇaprādurbhāvāttatsapatnīnāṃ kenaciccetanenādhiṣṭhātrā bhavitavyamtathā ca sarvārthadarśī parameśvaraḥ svīkattavyaḥ syāditi cet tadasaṃgatamacetanasyāpi pradhānasya prayojanavaśena pravṛttyupapatteḥdṛṣṭaṃ cācetanaṃ duḥkhaprahāṇecchānupapattiḥdvitīye parasparāśrayaprasaṅgaḥ karuṇayā sṛṣṭiḥ sṛṣṭyā ca kāruṇyamititasmādacetanasyāpi cetanānadhiṣṭhitasya pradhānasya mahadādirūpeṇa pariṇāmaḥ puruṣārthaprayuktaḥ pradhānapuruṣasaṃyoganimittaḥyathā nirvyāpārasyāpyayaskāntasya saṃnidhānena lohasya vyāpārastathā nirvyāpārasya puruṣasya saṃnidhānena pradhānavyāpāro yujyateprakṛtipuruṣasaṃbandhaśca paṅgvandhavatparasparāpekṣānibandhanaḥprakṛtirhi bhogyatayā bhoktāraṃ puruṣamapekṣatepuruṣopi bhedāgrahād buddhicchāyāpattyā tadgataṃ duḥkhatrayaṃ vārayamāṇaḥ kaivalyamapekṣatetat tpra sū  ityādinā yogalakṣaṇamabhidhāya samādhiṃ saprapañcaṃ niradikṣad bhagavānpatañjaliḥ dvitīye tapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni kriyāyogaḥ pāta yo sū  ityādinā vyutthitacittasya kriyāyogaṃ yamādīni ca paritapyamāne tadāropavaśena tadabhedāvagāhipuruṣopi tapyata ityucyatetaduktamācāryaiḥ  sattvaṃ tapyaṃ buddhibhāvena vṛttaṃ bhāvā ye vā rājasāstāpakāstetapyābhedagrāhiṇī tāmasī yā vṛttistasyāṃ tapya viṣayaḥtadvyutpādanamavāntaraphalamvyutpāditasya yogasya kaivalyaṃ paramaprayojanamśāstrayogayoḥ pratipādyapratipādakabhāvalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥyogasya kaivalyasya ca sādhyasādhanabhāvalakṣaṇaḥ saṃbandhaḥsa ca śrutyādiprasiddha iti prāgevāvādiṣammokṣamapekṣamāṇā evādhikāriṇa ityarthasiddhamna ca athāto brahmajijñāsā brasū ityādāvadhikāriṇorthataḥ siddhirāśaṅkanīyātatrāthaśabdenānantaryābhidhāna praṇāḍikayādhikārisamarpaṇasiddhāvārthikatvaśaṅkānudayātata evoktaṃ śrutiprāpte prakaraṇādīnāmanavakāśaḥ itiasyārthaḥ  yatra hi śrutyārthoṃ na labhyate tatraiva prakaraṇādayorthaṃ samarpayanti netaratrayatra tu śabdādevārthasyopalambhastatra netarasya saṃbhavaḥśīghrabodhinyā śrutyā viniyogasya bodhanena nirākāṅkṣatayetareṣāmanavakāśātkiṃ ca śrutyā bodhiterthaṃ tadviruddhārthe prakaraṇādi samarpayatyaviruddhaṃ vā na prathamaḥ viruddhārthabodhakasya tasya bādhitatvatna caramaḥ vaiyarthyāttadāha śrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ samavāye pāradaurbalyamarthaviprakarṣāt jaisū itibādhikaiva śrutirnityaṃ samākhyā bādhyate sadāmadhyamānāṃ tu bādhyatvaṃ bādhakatvamapekṣayā iti catasmādviṣayādimattvād brahmavicārakaśāstravad yogānuśāsanaṃ śāstramārambhaṇīyamiti sthitamnanu vyutpādyamānatayā yoga evātra prastuto na śāstramiti cet satyampratipādyatayā yogaḥ pradhānyena prastutaḥsa ca tadviṣayeṇa śāstreṇa pratipādyata iti tatpratipādane karaṇaṃ śāstramkaraṇagocaraśca kartṛvyāpāro na karmagocaratāmācaratiyathā chetturdevadattasya vyāpārabhūtamudyamana nipātanādikarma karaṇabhūtaparaśugocaraṃ na karmabhūtavṛkṣādigocaramtathā ca vaktuḥ yogaścittavṛttinirodha ityucyatenanu yujiryoṃga iti saṃyogārthatayā paripaṭhitādyujerniṣpanno yogaśabdaḥ saṃyogavacana eva syānna tu nirodhavacanaḥata evoktaṃ yājñavalkyena  saṃyogo yoga ityukto eva kecana yujiṃ samādhāvapi paṭhanti yuja samādhauitināpi yājñavalkyavacanavyākopaḥtatrasthasyāpi yogaśabdasya samādhyarthatvātsamādhiḥ samatāvasthā jīvātmaparamātmanoḥbrahmaṇyeva sthitiryā sā samādhiḥ pratyagātmanaḥ iti tenaivoktatvāccataduktaṃ bhagavatā vyāsena  yogabhā  yogaḥ samādhiritinanvevamaṣṭāṅgayoge caramasyāṅgasya samādhitvamuktaṃ patañjalinā pātayosū yamaniyamāsanaprāṇāyāmapratyāhāradhāraṇādhyānasamādhayoṣṭāvaṅgāni yogasya itina cāṅgyevāṅgatāṃ gantumutsahate upakāryopakārakabhāvasya darśapūrṇamāsaprayājādau bhinnāyatana tvenātyantabhedātataḥ samādhirapi na yogaśabdārthoṃ yujyata iti cet tanna yujyate vyutpattimātrābhidhitsayā tadevārthamātranirbhāsaṃ svarūpaśūnyamiva samādhiḥ pāta yo sū  iti nirūpitacaramāṅgavācake na samādhiśabdenāṅgino yogasyābhedavivakṣayā vyapadeśopapatteḥna ca vyutpattibalādeva sarvatra śabdaḥ pravartatetathātve gacchatīti gauriti vyutpattestiṣṭhangaurna syātgacchandevadattaśca gauḥ syātpravṛttinimittaṃ ca prāguktameva cittavṛttinirodha ititaduktaṃ yogaścittavṛttinirodhaḥ pāta yo sū  itinanu vṛttīnāṃ nirodhaścedyogobhimatastāsāṃ jñānatvenātmāśrayatayā tannirodhopi pradhvaṃsapadavedanīyastadāśrayo bhavet prāgabhāvapradhvaṃsayoḥ pratiyogisamānāśrayatvaniyamāttataśca  upayannapayandharmo vikaroti hi dharmiṇam iti nyāyenātmanaḥ kauṭasthyaṃ vihanyeteti cet tadapi na ghaṭate nirodhapratiyogibhūtānāṃ pramāṇaviparyayavikalpanidrāsmṛtisvarūpāṇāṃ vṛttīnāmantaḥkaraṇādyaparaparyāyacittadharmatvāṅgīkārātkūṭasthanityā cicchaktirapariṇāminī vijñānadharmāśrayo bhavituṃ nārhatyevana ca citiśakterapariṇāmitvamasiddhamiti mantavyam citiśaktirapariṇāminī sadā jñātṛtvāt na yadevaṃ na tadevaṃ yathā cittādi  ityādyanumānasaṃbhavāttathā yadyasau puruṣaḥ pariṇāmī syāttadā pariṇāmasya kādācitkatvāt tāsāṃ cittavṛttīnāṃ sadā jñātatvaṃ nopapadyetacidrūpasya puruṣasya sadaivādhiṣṭhātṛtvenāvasthitasya yadantaraṅgaṃ nirmalaṃ sattvaṃ tasyāpi sadaiva sthitatvāt yena yenārthenoparaktaṃ bhavati tasya dṛśyasya sadaiva cicchāyāpattyā bhānopapattyā puruṣasya niḥsaṅgatvaṃ saṃbhavatitataśca siddhaṃ tasya sadā jñātṛtvamiti na kadācitpariṇāmitvaśaṅkāvataraticittaṃ punaryena viṣayeṇoparaktaṃ bhavati sa viṣayo jñātaḥ yenoparaktaṃ na bhavati tadajñātamiti vastunoyaskāntamaṇikalpasya jñānājñānakāraṇabhūtoparāgānuparāgadharmitvādayaḥ sadharmakaṃ cittaṃ pariṇāmītyucyatenanu cittasyendriyāṇāṃ cāhaṃkārikāṇāṃ sarvagatatvāsarvaviṣayairasti sadā saṃbandhaḥtathā ca sarveṣāṃ sarvadā savatra jñānaṃ prasajyeteti cet  na sarvagatatvepi cittaṃ yatra śarīre vṛttimat tena śarīreṇa saha saṃbandho yeṣāṃ viṣayāṇāṃ teṣvevāsya jñānaṃ bhavati netareṣvityatiprasaṅgābhāvātata evāyaskāntamaṇikalpā viṣayā ayaḥsadharmakaṃ cittamindriyapraṇālikayābhisaṃbandhyopa rañjayantītyuktamtasmāccittasya dharmā vṛttayo nātmanaḥtathā ca śrutiḥ  kāmaḥ saṃkalpo vicikitsā śraddhāśraddhādhṛtiradhṛtirhrīrdhīrbhīrityetatsarvaṃ mana eva bṛ  iticicchakterapariṇāmitvaṃ pañcaśikhācāryairākhyāyi aparaṇāminī bhoktṛśaktiḥ itipatañjalināpi  sadā jñātāścittavṛttayastatprabhoḥ puruṣasyāpariṇāmitvāt pātayosū  iticittapariṇāmitvenumānamucyate  cittaṃ pariṇāmi jñātājñātaviṣayatvāt śrotrādivaditipariṇāmaśca trividhaḥ prasiddho dharmalakṣaṇāvasthābhedātdharmiṇaścittasya nīlādyālocanaṃ dharmapariṇāmaḥ yathā kanakasya kaṭakamukuṭakeyūrādidharmasya vartamānatvādirlakṣaṇapariṇāmaḥnīlādyālocanasya sphuṭatvādiravasthāpariṇāmaḥkaṭakādestu navapurāṇatvādiravasthāpariṇāmaḥevamanyatrāpi yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pariṇāmatritayamūhanīyamtathā ca pramāṇadivṛttīnāṃ cittadharmatvātta nnirodhopi tadāśraya eveti na kiṃcidanupapannamnanu vṛttinirodho yoga ityaṅgīkāre suṣuptayādau kṣiptamūḍhādicittavṛttīnāṃ nirodhasaṃbhavādyogatvaprasaṅgaḥna caitadyujyate kṣiptādyavasthāsu kleśaprahāṇāderasaṃbhavānniḥ śreyasaparipanthitvāccatathā hi kṣiptaṃ nāma teṣu teṣu viṣayeṣu kṣipyamāṇamasthiraṃ cittamucyatetamaḥsamudre magnaṃ nidrāvṛttibhāvitaṃ mūḍhamiti gīyatekṣiptādviśiṣṭaṃ cittaṃ vikṣiptamiti gīyateviśeṣo nāma cañcalaṃ hi manaḥ kṛṣṇa pramāthi balavad dṛḍham gī iti nyāyenāsthirasyāpi manasaḥ kādācitkasamudbhūtaviṣayasthairyasaṃbhavena sthairyamasthiratvaṃ ca svābhāvikaṃ vyādhyādyanuśayajanitaṃ vātadāha vyādhistyānasaṃśayapramādālasyāviratibhrāntidarśanālabdha bhūmikatvānavasthitatvāni cittavikṣepāstentarāyāḥ pāta yo sū ititatra doṣatrayavaiṣamyanimitto jvarādirvyādhiḥcittasyākarmaṇyatvaṃ styānamviruddhakoṭidvayāvagāhi jñānaṃ saṃśayaḥsamādhisādhanānāmabhāvanaṃ pramādaḥśarīravākcittagurutvādapravṛttirālasyamviṣayābhilāṣoviratiḥatasmiṃstadbuddhi bhrāntidarśanamkutaścinnimittātsamādhibhūmeralābholabdhabhūmikatvamlabdhāyāmapi tasyāṃ cittasyāpratiṣṭhānavasthitatvamityarthaḥtasmānna vṛttinirodho yogapakṣanikṣepamarhatīti cet maivaṃ vocaḥ heyabhūtakṣiptādyavasthātraye vṛttinirodhasya yogatvāsaṃbhavepyupādeyayorekāgraniruddhā vasthayorvṛttinirodhasya yogatvasaṃbhavātekatānaṃ cittamekāgramucyateniruddhasakalavṛttikaṃ saṃskāramātraśeṣaṃ cittaṃ niruddhamiti bhaṇyatesa ca samādhirddhividhaḥsaṃprajñātāsaṃprajñātabhedāttatraikāgracetasi yaḥ pramāṇādivṛttīnāṃ bāhyaviṣayāṇāṃ nirodhaḥ sa saṃprajñātaḥ samādhiḥ samyakprajñāyatesminprakṛterviviktatayā dhyeyamiti vyutpatteḥsa caturvidhaḥ savitarkādibhedātsamādhirnāma bhāvanāsā ca bhāvyasya viṣayāntaraparihāreṇa cetasi punaḥ punarniveśanambhāvyaṃ ca dvividham īśvarastattvāni catānyapi dvividhāni jaḍājaḍabhedātjaḍāni prakṛtimahadahaṃkārādīni caturviṃśatiḥajaḍaḥ puruṣaḥtatra tadā pṛthivyādīni sthūlāni viṣayatvenādāya pūrvāparānusaṃdhānena śabdārthollekhasaṃbhedena ca bhāvanā pravartate sa samādhiḥ savitarkaḥyadā tanmātrāntaḥkaraṇalakṣaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ viṣayamālambya deśādyavacchedena bhāvanā pravartate tadā savicāraḥyadā rajastamoleśānuviddhaṃ cittaṃ bhāvyate tadā sukhaprakāśamayasya sattvasyodrekātsānandaḥyadā rajastamoleśānabhibhūtaṃ śuddhaṃ sattvamālambanīkṛtya yā pravartate bhāvanā tadā tasyāṃ sattvasya nyagbhāvāccitiśakterudrekācca sattāmātrāvaśeṣatvena sāsmitaḥ samādhiḥtaduktaṃ patañjalināvitarka vicārānandāsmitārupānugamātsaṃprajñātaḥ pāta yo sū  itisarvavṛttinirodhe tvasaṃprajñātaḥ samādhiḥnanu sarvavṛttinirodho yoga ityukte saṃprajñāte vyāptirna syāt tatra sattvapradhānāyāḥ sattvapuruṣānyatākhyātilakṣaṇāyāṃ vṛtteranirodhāditi cet  tadetadvārtam kleśakarmavipākāśayaparipanthicittavṛttinirodho yoga ityaṅgīkārātkleśāḥ punaḥ pañcadhā prasiddhāḥ avidyāsmitārāgadveṣābhiniveśāḥ kleśāḥ pātayosūitinanvavidyetyatra kimāśrīyate pūrvapadārthaprādhānyamamakṣikaṃ vartata itivatuttarapadārthaprādhānyaṃ vā rājapuruṣa itivat anyapadārthaprādhānyaṃ vā amakṣiko deśa itivattatra na pūrvaḥ pūrvapadārthapradhānatve avidyāyāṃ prasajyapratiṣedhopapattau kleśādikārakatvānupapatteḥ avidyāśabdasya strīliṅgatvābhāvāpatteścana dvitīyaḥ kasyacidabhāvena viśiṣṭāyā vidyāyāḥ kleśādiparipanthitvena tadbījatvānupapatteḥna tṛtīyaḥ nañostyarthānāṃ bahuvrīhirvā cottarapadalopaśca iti vṛttikāravacanānusāreṇāvidyamānā vidyā yasyāḥ sā avidyā buddhiriti samāsārthasiddhau tasyā avidyāyāḥ kleśadibījatvānupapatteḥ vivekakhyātipūrvakasarvavṛttinirodhasaṃpannāyāstasyā stathātvaprasaṅgāccauktaṃ cāsmitādīnāṃ kleśānāmavidyānidānatvam avidyā kṣetramuttāreṣāṃ prasuptatanuvicchinnodārāṇām pātayosū itiprasuptatvaṃ prabodhasahakāryabhāvenānabhivyaktiḥtanutvaṃ pratipakṣabhāvanayā śithilīkaraṇamvicchinnatvaṃ balavatā kleśenābhibhavaḥudāratvaṃ sahakāri saṃnidhivaśātkāryakāritvamtaduktaṃ vācaspatimiśreṇa vyāsabhāṣyavyākhyāyām prasuptāstattvalīnānāṃ tanvavasthāśca yogināmvicchinnodārarupāśca kleśā viṣayasaṅginām itidvandvavatsvatantrapadārthadvayānavagamādubhayapadārthapradhānatvaṃ nāśaṅkitamtasmātpakṣatrayepi kleśādi nidānatvamavidyāyāḥ prasiddhaṃ hīyeteti cet  tadapi na śobhanaṃ vibhāti paryudāsaśaktimāśrityāvidyāśabdena vidyāviruddhasya viparyayajñānasyābhi bhidhānamiti vṛddhairaṅgīkārāttadāha nāmadhātvarthayoge tu naiva nañ pratiṣedhakaḥvadatyabrāhmaṇādharmāvanyamātravirodhinau itivṛddhaprayogagamyo hi śabdārthaḥ sarva eva naḥtena yatra prayukto yo na tasmādapanīyate itivācaspatimiśrairapyuktam  lokādhīnāvadhāraṇo hi śabdārthayoḥ saṃbandhaḥloke cottarapadārthapradhānasyāpi naña uttarapadābhidheyopamardakasya tadviruddhatayā tatra tatropalabdherihāpi tadviruddhe pravṛttiḥitietadevābhipretyoktam anityāśuciduḥkhānātmasu nityaśucisukhātmakhyātiravidyā pātasū itiatasmiṃstadbuddhirviparyaya ityuktaṃ bhavatitadyathā anitye ghaṭādau nityatvābhimānaḥaśucau kāyādau śucitvapratyayaḥ sthānādvījādapaṣṭambhānniṣyandānnidhanādupikāyamādheyaśaucatvātpaṇḍitā hyaśuciṃ viduḥ pariṇāmatāpasaṃskāraduḥkhairguṇavṛttyavirodhācca duḥkhameva sarvaṃ vivekinaḥ pāta yo sū  iti nyāyena duḥkhe srakcandanavanitādau sukhatvāropaḥanātmani dehādāvātmabuddhiḥtaduktam  anātmani ca dehādāvātmabuddhistu dehināmavidyā tatkṛto bandhastannāśo mokṣa ucyateevamiyamavidyā catuṣpadā bhavatinanveteṣvavidyāviśeṣeṣu kiṃcidanugataṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ varṇanīyam anyathā viśeṣasyāsiddheḥtathā coktaṃ bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ  sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ muktvā viśeṣasyaiva lakṣaṇamna śakyaṃ kevalaṃ vaktumatopyasya na vācyatātadapi na vācyamatasmiṃstadbuddhiriti sāmānyalakṣaṇābhidhānena dattottaratvātsattvapuruṣayorahamasmītyekatābhimānosmitātadapyuktaṃ dṛgdarśanaśaktyorekātmatevāsmitā pātayosū itisukhābhijñasya sukhānusmṛtipūrvakaḥ sukhasādhaneṣu tṛṣṇārūpo gardhoṃ rāgaḥduḥkhābhijñasya tadanusmṛtipurassaraṃ tatsādhaneṣu nivṛttirdveṣaḥtaduktaṃ  sukhānuśayī rāgaḥ pātayosū duḥkhānuśayī dveṣaḥ pātayosū itikimatrānuśayiśabde tācchīlyārthe ṇinirinirvā matvarthīyobhimataḥ nādyaḥ supyajātau ṇinistācchīlye pāsū ityatra supīti vartamāne punaḥ subgrahaṇasyopasarganivṛttyarthatvena sopasargāddhātorṇineranutpatteḥyathākathaṃcittadaṅgīkārepi aco ñṇiti pāsū iti vṛddhiprasaktāvatiśāyyādipadavadanuśāyipadasya prayogaprasaṅgātna dvitīyaḥ ekākṣarātkṛto jāteḥ saptamyāṃ ca na tau smṛtau iti tatpratiṣedhāt atra cānuśayaśabdasyājantatvena kṛdantatvāttasmādanuśayiśabdo darupapāda iti cet naitadbhadram bhāvānavabodhātprāyikābhiprāyamidaṃ vacanamata evoktaṃ vṛttikāreṇa  itikaraṇo vivakṣārthaḥ sarvatrābhisaṃbadhyate ititena kvacidbhavati kāryī kāryikastaṇḍulī taṇḍulikaḥ ititathā ca kṛdantājjāteścapratiṣedhasya prāyikatvamanuśayaśabdasya kṛdantatayenerupapattiriti siddhampūrvajanmānubhūtamaraṇaduḥkhānubhavavāsanābalātsarvasya prāṇabhṛnmātrasyākṛmerā ca viduṣaḥ saṃjāyamānaḥ śarīraviṣayādermama viyogo mā bhūditi pratyahaṃ nimittaṃ vinā pravartamāno bhayarūpobhiniveśaḥ prañcamaḥ kleśaḥ mā na bhūvaṃ hi bhūyāsamiti prārthanāyāḥ pratyātmamanubhavasiddhatvāttadāhasvarasavāhī viduṣopi tathā rūḍhobhiniveśaḥ pātayosū itite cāvidyādayaḥ pañca sāṃsārikavividhaduḥkhopahārahetutvena puruṣaṃ kliśnantīti kleśāḥ prasiddhāḥkarmāṇi vihitapratiṣiddharūpāṇi jyotiṣṭomabrahmahatyādīnivipākāḥ karmaphalāni jātyāyurbhoṃgāḥā phalavipākāccittabhūmau śerata ityāśayā dharmādharmasaṃskārāḥtatparipanthicittāvṛttinirodho yogaḥnirodho nābhāvamātramabhimatam tasya tucchatvena bhāvarūpasākṣātkārajananakṣamatvāsaṃbhavātkiṃ tu tadāśrayo madhumatīmadhupratīkāviśokāsaṃskāraśeṣāvyapadeśyaścittasyāvasthāviśeṣaḥ nirudhyantesmin pramāṇādyāścittavṛttaya iti vyutpatterūpapatteḥabhyāsavairāgyābhyāṃ vṛttinirodhaḥtatra sthitau yatnobhyāsaḥpātayosū vṛttirahitasya cittasya svarūpaniṣṭhaḥ praśāntavāhitārūpaḥ pariṇāmaviroṣaḥ sthitiḥtaṃ nimittīkṛtya yatnaḥ punaḥ punastathātvena cetasi niveśanamabhyāsaḥcarmaṇi dvīpinaṃ hantiitivannimittārtheyaṃ saptamītyuktaṃ bhavatidṛṣṭānuśravikaviṣayavitṛṣṇasya vaśīkārasaṃjñā vairāgyam  pāta yo sū aihikapāratrikaviṣayādau doṣadarśanānnirabhilāṣasya mamaite viṣayā vaśyāḥ nāhameteṣāṃ vaśyaḥ iti vimarśoṃ vairāgyamityuktaṃ bhavatisamādhiparipanthikleśatanūkaraṇārthaṃ samādhilābhārthaṃ ca prathamaṃ kriyāyogavidhānapareṇa yoginā bhavitavyam kriyāyogasaṃpādanebhyāsavairāgyayoḥ saṃbhavāttaduktaṃ bhagavatā  ārurukṣormuneryoṃgaṃ karma kāraṇamucyateyogāruḍhasya tasyaiva śamaḥ kāraṇamucyate bhagī itikriyāyogaścopadiṣṭaḥ patañjalinā tapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni kriyāyogaḥ pāta yo sū  ititapaḥsvarūpaṃ nirupitaṃ yājñavalakyena vidhinokte na mārgeṇa kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥśarīraśoṣaṇaṃ prāhustapasāṃ tapa uttamam itipraṇavagāyatrīprabhṛtīnāṃ mantrāṇāmadhyayanaṃ svādhyāyaḥte ca mantrā dvividhāḥ vaidikāstāntrikāścavaidikāśca dvividhāḥpragītāḥ apragītāścatatra pragītāḥ sāmāniapragītāśca dvividhāḥ chandobaddhāstadvilakṣaṇāścatatra prathamā ṛco dvitīyā yajūṃṣitaduktaṃ jaimininā teṣāmṛgyatrārthavaśena pādavyavasthāgītiṣu sāmākhyāśeṣe yajuḥśabdaḥ jaisū ititantreṣu kāmikakāraṇaprapañcādyāgameṣu ye ye varṇitāste tāntrikāḥte punarmantrāstrividhāḥ strīpuṃnapuṃsakabhedāttadāha  strīpuṃnapuṃsakatvena trividhā mantrajātayaḥstrīmantrā vahnijāyāntā namontāḥ syurnapuṃsakāḥśeṣāḥ pumāṃsaste śastāḥ siddhā vaśyādikarmaṇi itijananādisaṃskārābhāvepi nirastasamastadoṣatvena siddhihetutvātsiddhatvamsa ca saṃskāro daśavidhaḥ kathitaḥ śāradātilake  mantrāṇāṃ daśa kathyante saṃskārāḥ siddhidāyinaḥnirdoṣatāṃ prayāntyāśu te mantrāḥ sādhu saṃskṛtāḥjananaṃ jīvanaṃ caiva tāḍanaṃ bodhanaṃ tathāabhiṣekotha vimalīkaraṇāpyāyane punaḥtarpaṇaṃ dīpanaṃ gaptirdaśaitā mantrasaṃskriyāḥmantrāṇāṃ mātṛkāyantrāduddhāro jananaṃ smṛtampraṇavāntaritānkṛtvā mantravarṇāñjapetsudhīḥmantrārṇasaṃkhyayā taddhi jīvanaṃ saṃpracakṣatemantravarṇānsamālikhya tāḍayeccandanāmbhasāpratyekaṃ vāyubījena tāḍanaṃ tadudāhṛtamvilikhya mantravarṇāṃstu prasūnaiḥ karavīrajaiḥmantrākṣareṇa saṃkhyātairhanyāttadvodhanaṃ smṛtamsvatantroktavidhānena mantrī mantrārṇasaṃkhyayāaśvatthapallavairmantramabhiṣiñcedviśuddhayesaṃcintya manasā mantraṃ jyotirmantreṇa nirdahetmantre malatrayaṃ mantrī vimalīkaraṇaṃ hi tattāravyomāgni manuyugjyotirmantra udāhṛtaḥkuśodakena japtena pratyarṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥvārivījena vidhivadetadāpyāyanaṃ matammantreṇa vāriṇā mantre tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ smṛtamtāramāyāramāyogo manordīpanamucyatejapyamānasya mantrasya gopanaṃ tvaprakāśanamsaṃskārā daśa mantrāṇāṃ sarvatantreṣu gopitāḥyatkṛtvā saṃpradāyena mantrī vāñchitamaśnuteruddhakīlitavicchinna suptaśaptādayopi camantradoṣāḥ praṇaśyanti saṃskārairebhiruttamaiḥtadalamakāṇḍatāṇḍavakalpena mantraśāstrarahasyoddhoṣaṇenaīśvarapraṇidhānaṃ nāmābhihitānāmanabhihitānāṃ ca sarvāsāṃ kriyāṇāṃ parameśvare paramagurau phalānapekṣayā  samarpaṇamyatredamuktam  kāmatokāmato vāpi yatkaromi śubhāśubhamtatsarvaṃ tvayi vinyastaṃ tvatprayuktaḥ karomyahamkriyāphalasaṃnyāsopi bhaktiviśeṣāparaparyāyaṃ praṇidhānameva phalānabhisaṃdhānena karmakāraṇāttathā ca gīyate gītāsu bhagavatā  karmaṇyevādhikāraste mā phaleṣu kadācanamā karmaphalaheturbhūrmā te saṅgostvakarmaṇibhagī itiphalābhisaṃdherupaghātakatvamabhihitaṃ bhagavadbhirnīlakaṇṭhabhāratīśrīcaraṇaiḥ  api prayatnasaṃpannaṃ kāmenopahataṃ tapaḥna tuṣṭaye maheśasya śvalīḍhamiva pāyasamsā ca tapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānātmikā kriyā yogasādhanatvādyoga iti śuddhasāropalakṣaṇā vṛttyāśrayaṇena nirupyate yathāyurghṛtamitiśuddhasāropalakṣaṇā nāma śuddhasādhyavasānā cetikuntāḥ praviśanti mañcāḥ kośanti gaurvāhīkaḥ gaurayam āyurghṛtam āyurevedam iti yathākramamudāharaṇāni draṣṭavyānitaduktam  svasiddhaye parākṣepaḥ parārthaṃ śuddhau ca vijñeyau lakṣaṇā tena ṣaḍvidhākāpra ititadalaṃ kāvyamīmāṃsāmarmanirmanthanenasa ca yogo yamādibhedavaśādaṣṭāṅga iti nirdiṣṭaḥtatra yamā ahiṃsādayaḥtadāha patañjaliḥ ahiṃsāsatyāsteyabrahmacaryāparigrahā yamāḥpāta yo sū  itiniyamāḥ śaicādayaḥtadapyāhaśaucasaṃtoṣatapaḥsvādhyāyeśvarapraṇidhānāni niyamāḥ pāta yo sū  itiete ca yamaniyamā viṣṇupurāṇe darśitāḥbrahmacaryamāhiṃsāṃ ca satyāsteyāparigrahānseveta yogī niṣkāmo yogyatāṃ svaṃ mano nayansvādhyāyaśaucasaṃtoṣatapāṃsi niyatātmavānkurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasminpravaṇaṃ manaḥete yamāḥ saniyamāḥ pañca pañca prakīrtitāḥviśiṣṭaphaladāḥ kāme niṣkāmāṇāṃ vimuktidāḥvipu itisthirasukhamāsanaṃ pātayosū padmāsanabhadrāsanavīrāsanasvastikāsanadaṇḍakāsanasopāśraya svaviṣayāsaṃprayoge cittasvarūpānukāra ivendriyāṇāṃ pratyāhāraḥ pā yo sū  itisādṛśyaṃ ca cittānukāranimittaṃ viṣayāsaṃprayogaḥyadā cittaṃ nirudhyate tadā cakṣurādīnāṃ nirodhe prayatnāntaraṃ guṇapariṇāmarūpāṇāṃ bhāvānāṃ svāmivadākramaṇaṃ sarvabhāvādhiṣṭhātṛtvamteṣāmeva śāntoditāvyapadeśyadharmitvena sthitānāṃ vivekajñānaṃ sarvajñātṛtvamtaduktaṃ viśokā vā jyotiṣmatī pātayosū kuṅkumapaṅkaḥ sukho bhavetna hyasau kadācidakuṅkumapaṅka itievaṃ kaṇṭakaḥ kramelakasyeva manuṣyādīnāmapi prāṇabhṛtāṃ sukhaḥ syātna hyasau kāṃścitpratyeva kaṇṭaka ititasmāccandanakuṅkumādayo viśeṣāḥ tadapāṃ yatkṛṣṇaṃ tadannasya chā iti cchāndogyaśākhāyāṃ tejobannātmikāyāḥ prakṛterlohitaśuklakṛṣṇarūpāṇi samāmnātāni tānyevātra pratyabhijñāyantetatra śrautapratyabhijñāyāḥ prābalyāllohitādiśabdānāṃ mukhyārthasaṃbhavācca tejobannātmikā jarāyujāṇḍaja svedajodbhijjacatuṣṭayasya bhūtagrāmasya prakṛtiravasīyateyadyapi tejobannānāṃ prakṛterjātatvena yogavṛttyā na jāyata ityajatvaṃ na sidhyati tathāpi ruḍhivṛttyāvagatamajātvamuktaprakṛtau sukhāvabodhāya prakalpyateyathā asau vādityo devamadhu chā ityādivākyenādityasya madhutvaṃ parikalpyate tathā tejobannātmikā prakṛtirevājetiatojāmekāmityādikā śrutirapi na pradhānapratipādikāyadavādi nidarśanaṃ pūrvavādinā kṣīrādikamacetanaṃ cetanānadhiṣṭhitameva vatsavivṛddhayarthaṃ pravartata itinaitadramaṇīyambuddhiviśeṣaśālinaḥ parameśvarasya tatrāpyadhiṣṭhātṛtvābhyupagamātna ca parameśvarasya karuṇayā pravṛttyaṅgīkāre prāguktavikalpāvasaraḥsṛṣṭeḥ prāk prāṇināṃ duḥkhasaṃbandhāsaṃbhavepi tannidānādṛṣṭasaṃbandhasaṃbhavena tatprahāṇecchayā pravṛttyupapatteḥkiṃ ca puruṣārthaprayuktā pradhānapravṛttirityuktaṃ tadvivektavyamkiṃ pradhānaṃ ke valaṃ bhogārthe pravartatekiṃ vā ke valamokṣārtha māhosvidubhayārthamna tāvadādyaḥ vidadhyānna mokṣamitināpi dvitīyaḥciddhātornityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvatayā karmānubhavavāsanānāmasaṃbhavena pradhānapravṛtteḥ prāgapi muktatayā tadarthaṃ pravṛttyanupapatteḥśabdādyupabhogārthamapravṛttattvena pradhānasya tadajanakatvaprasaṅgāccanāpi tṛtīyaḥprāguktadūṣaṇalaṅghanālaṅghitatvātpravṛttisvabhāvāyāḥ prakṛteraudāsīnyāyogāccananu sattvapuruṣānyathākhyātiḥ puruṣārthaḥtasyāṃ jātāyāṃ sā nivartate kṛtakāryatvāditi cet tadasamañjasamacetanāyāḥ prakṛtervicārya kāryakāritvāyogātyatheyaṃ kṛtepi śabdādyupalambhe tadarthaṃ punaḥ pravartata evamatrāpi punaḥ pravartetasvabhāvasyānapāyātkiṃ ca sā prakṛtirvivekakhyātivaśāducchidyate na vāucchede sarvasya saṃprati saṃsārostamiyātanucche de na kasyacinmokṣaḥnanu pradhānābhedepi tattatpuruṣāvivekakhyātilakṣaṇavidyāsadasattvanibandhanau bandhamokṣāvupapadyeyātāmiti cet hanta tarhi kṛtaṃ prakṛtyāavidyāsadasadbhāvābhyāmeva tadupapatteḥnanvavidyāpakṣepyeṣa doṣaḥ prāduḥṣyāditi cet tadetatpratyavasthānamasthānena hi vayaṃ pradhānavadavidyāṃ sarveṣu jīveṣvekāmācakṣmahe yenaivamupālabhyemahiapi tviyaṃ pratijīvaṃ bhidyatetena yasyaiva jīvasya vidyotpadyate tasyaivāvidyāsamucchidyate nānyasyabhinnāyatanayostayo rvirodhābhāvātato na samastasaṃsārocche daprasaṅgadoṣaḥtasmātpariṇāmaḥ parityaktavyaḥsvīkartavyaśca vivartavādaḥnanu jīvajaḍayoḥ sārūpyābhāvena cidvivartatvaṃ prapañcasya na saṃparipadyate iti prāgavādiṣmeti cet naitatsādhuna hi sārūpyanibandhanāḥ sarve vibhramā iti vyāptirastiasarupādapi kāmādeḥ kāntāliṅganādiṣviva svapnavibhramasyopalambhātkiṃ ca kādācitke vibhrame sārūpyāpekṣā nānādyavidyānibandhane prapañcetadavocadācāryavācaspatiḥvivartastu prapañcoyaṃ brahmaṇopiriṇāminaḥanādivāsanodbhūto na sārūpyamapekṣatetadevatsarvaṃ vedāntaśāstrapariśramaśālināṃ sugamaṃ sughaṭaṃ catacca vedāntaśāstraṃ caturlakṣaṇambhagavatā bādarāyaṇena praṇītasya vedāntaśāstrasya pratyagbrahmaikyaṃ viṣaya iti śaṃkarācāryāḥ pratyapīpadantatra prathame samanvayādhyāye sarveṣāṃ vedāntānāṃ brahmaṇi tātparyeṇa paryavasānamdvitīyevirodhādhyāye sāṃkhyāditarka virodha nirākaraṇamtṛtīye sādhanādhyāye vrahmavidyāsādhanamcaturthe phalādhyāye vidyāphalamtatra pratyadhyāyaṃ pādacatuṣṭayamtatra prathamasyādhyāyasya prathame pāde spaṣṭabrahmaliṅgaṃ vākyajātaṃ mīmāṃsyatedvitīyespaṣṭabrahmaliṅga mupāsyaviṣayamtṛtīye tādṛśaṃ jñeyaviṣayamcaturthevyaktājāpadādi saṃdigdhaṃ padajātamitiavirodhasya dvitīyasya prathame sāṃkhyayogakaṇādādismṛtivirodhaparihāraḥdvitīye sāṃkhyādimatānāṃ duṣṭatvamtṛtīye pañcamahābhūtaśrutīnāṃ jīvaśrutīnāṃ ca parasparavirodhaparihāraḥcaturthe liṅgaśarīraśrutīnāṃ virodhaparihāraḥtṛtīyasya prathame jīvasya paralokagamanāgamanavicārapuraḥsaraṃ vairāgyamdvitīye tvaṃpadatatpadārthapariśodhanamtṛtīye saguṇavidyāsu guṇopasaṃhāraḥcaturthe nirguṇabrahmavidyāyā bahiraṃgāntaraṃgāśramayajñaśamādisādhanajātamcaturthasya prathame brahmasākṣātkāreṇa jīvataḥ pāpapuṇyakleśavaidhuryalakṣaṇā muktiḥdvitīye maraṇotkramaṇaprakāraḥtṛtīye saguṇabrahmopāsakasyottaramārgaḥcaturthe nirguṇasaguṇabrahmavido videhakai valyabrahmalokāvasthānānitaditthaṃ brahmavicāraśāstrādhyāyapādārthasaṃgrahaḥtatra prathamamadhikaraṇamathāto brahmajijñāsā vrasū iti brahmamīmāṃsārambhopapādanaparamadhikaraṇaṃ ca pañcāvayavaṃ prasiddhamte ca viṣayādayaḥ pañcāvayavā nirūpyanteātmā vāre draṣṭavyaḥ bṛ ityetadvākyaṃ viṣayaḥbrahma jijñāsitavyaṃ na veti saṃdehaḥjijñāsyatvavyāpakayoḥ saṃdehaprayojanayoḥ saṃbhavāsaṃbhavābhyāmtatra kasyedaṃ jijñāsyatvamavagamyateahamanubhavagamyasya śrutigamyasya vānādyaḥsarvajanīnenāhamanubhavenedamāspadadehādibhyo viveke nātmanaḥ spaṣṭaṃ pratibhāsamānatvātnanu sthūlohaṃ kṛśohamityādidehadharmasāmānādhikaraṇyānubhavādadhyastātmabhāvadehālambanoyamahaṃkāra iti cennabālyādyavasthāsu bhinnaparimāṇatayā badarāmalakādivatparasparabhedena śarīrasya pratyabhijñānānupapatteḥathocceta yathā pīlupākapakṣe piṭharapākapakṣe vā kālabhedenaikāsminvastuni pākajabhedo yujyate tathaikasmiñśarīrābhidhe vastuni kālabhedena parimāṇabhedaḥata eva laukikāḥ śarīramātmanaḥ sakāśādabhinnaṃ pratipadyamānāḥ pratyabhijānate cetina tadbhadrammaṇimantrauṣadhādyupāyabhedena bhūmikādhānavannānāvidhāndehānpratipadyamānasyāhamālambanasya bhinnasyātmanaḥ śarīrādbhedena bhāsamānatvātata eva cakṣurādīnāmapyahamālambanatvamaśakyaśaṅkamnānyadṛṣṭaṃ smaratyanyaḥ nyāku su  iti nyāyena cakṣurādau naṣṭepi rūpādipratisaṃdhānānupapatteḥnāpyantaḥkaraṇasyāhamālambanatvamāstheyamayameva bhedo bhedaheturvā yadviruddhadharmādhyāsaḥ kāraṇabhedaśceti nyāyena kartṛkaraṇabhūtayorātmāntaḥkaraṇayostakṣavāsivatsaṃbhedāsaṃbhavātyadyabhedaeva nādriyate tarhi sthūlohaṃ kṛśohaṃ kṛṣṇohamityādi saṃkhyānamutsannasaṃkathaṃ syātna syātevaṃ loke śāstre cobhayathā śabda prayogadarśanena mukhyārthatvānupapattau mañcāḥ krośantītyādivadaupacārikatvenopapatteḥna dvitīyaḥahamanubhavagamyasyaiva śrutigamyatvātsatyaṃ jñānamanantaṃ brahma tai ityādiśrutibhyo hi brahmāvagamyatebrahmabhāvaścāhamātmā brahma bṛ tattvamasi chā ityādiśrutiṣvahaṃpratyaya gamyasyaiva bodhyatetathā cedamanumānaṃ samasūcivimatamajijñāsyamasaṃdigdhatvātkaratalāmalakavattathā phalaṃ na phalabhāvamīkṣatepuruṣairarthyata iti vyutpattyā niḥśeṣaduḥkhopaśamalakṣitaṃ paramānandaikarasaṃ ca puruṣārthaśabdasyārthaḥ sakalapuruṣadhaureyaiḥ prepsyate naitatsāṃsārikaṃ sukhajātamtasyaihikasya pāralaukikasya ca sātiśayatayā ca sadṛkṣatayā ca prekṣāvadbhirarthyamānatvānupapatteḥyattatparipanthi duḥkhajātaṃ tajjihāsyatetaccāvidyāparaparyāyasaṃsāra evakartṛtvādisakalānarthaka phalavatāmabhimatamtathā kathitam  avidyāstamayomokṣaḥ sā ca bandha udāhṛtaḥtacca kāśaku śāvalambanakalpamātmayāthātmyānubhavena saha vartamānasya saṃsārasya rūparasavadvirodhābhāvena nivartyanivartakabhāvābhāvātnanu sahānuvartamāno bodhaḥ saṃsāraṃ mā bādhiṣṭasahāvartamānastu bodhaḥ prakāśastamovadvādhiṣyata iti cet tadetadriktaṃ vacaḥahamanubhavādanyasyātmajñānasya mūṣikaviṣāṇāyamānatvātnanvanyoyamanubhavaḥ pāmarāṇāṃ mā sma bhavannāmavedāntavacananicayaparyālocanakṣamāṇāṃ parīkṣakāṇāṃ saṃbhavatyevetyapi na vaktavyamabādhitānubhavavirodhena vedāntavākyānāṃ grāvaplavanādivākyakalpatvātna hyāgamāḥ paraḥśataṃ ghaṭaṃ paṭayitumutsahantena cādhyayanavidhivyākopaḥgurumatānusāreṇa huṃphaḍādivākyavajja  pamātropayogitvenācāryamatānusāreṇa vā yajamānaḥ prastara ityādivākyavatstāvakatvena vedāntasiddhāntasyādhyetavyatvasaṃbhavāttathā ca prayogaḥ  vivādāspadaṃ brahma vicāryapadaṃ na bhavatyaphalatvātkākadantavadititadāhurācāryāḥ  ahaṃdhiyātmanaḥ siddhestasyaiva brahmabhāvataḥtajjñānānmuktyabhāvāśca jijñāsā nāvakalpatena ca bhedenādhyastadehādinivṛttiḥ phalamityaphalatvaheturasiddha iti veditavyambhedagraho hi vyāpakanivṛttyā vyāpyanivṛttiriti nyāyena bhedāgrahaparipanthinaṃ bhedasaṃskāramapekṣateanākalitakaladhautasya śuktiśakale tatsamāropānupalambhātsaṃskāraśca pramitimākāṅkṣatiananubhūte saṃskārānudayātna ca cātmānātmanorabhedāyogyatvalakṣaṇo heturasiddha iti śaṅkanīyamvikalpāsahatvāttathā hi ānātmātmapariśeṣaḥ syādātmānātmapariśeṣo vāādye muktidaśāyāmiva paridṛśyamānaṃ jagadastamiyātdvitīye jagadāndhyaṃ prasajyetatamaḥ prakāśavadviruddhasvabhāvatvācca dṛgdṛśyayorātmānātmanorabhedāyogyatvamavadheyamtataścārthādhyā sānupapattau tatpūrvakasya jñānādhyāsasyāsaṃbhavena brahmaṇo vicāryatvāsaṃbhavādvicārātmikā caturlakṣaṇaśārīrakamīmāṃsā nārambhaṇīyeti pūrvapakṣe prāpte siddhāntobhidhīyate  ahaṃpadādhigamyādanyadātmatattvaṃ nāstīti na vaktavyamnirastasamastopādhikasyātmatattvasya śrutyādiṣu prasiddhatvātna ca teṣāmupacaritārthatāupakramopasaṃhārādiṣaḍvighatātparyaliṅgavattayā tattvaṃ bodhayatāmupacaritārthatvānupapatteḥliṅgaṣaṭkaṃ ca pūrvācāryairdarśitam  upakramopasaṃhārāvabhyāsopūrvatā phalamarthavādopapattī ca liṅgaṃ tātparyanirṇayetatra sadeva saumyedamagra āsīdityupakramaḥaitadātmyamidaṃ sarvaṃ tatsatyaṃ sa ātmā tattvamasi śvetake to ityupasaṃhāraḥtayorbrahmaviṣayatvenaikyarūpyamekaliṅgamasakṛttattvamasītyuktirabhyāsaḥmānāntarāgamyatvamapūrvatvamekavijñānena sarvavijñānaṃ phalamsṛṣṭisthitipralayapraveśa niyamānāni pañcārthavādāḥmṛdādidṛṣṭāntā upapattayaḥtasmādetairliṅgairvedāntānāṃ nityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvabrahmātmaparatvaṃ niścetavyamtaditthamaupaniṣadasyātmatattvasyāhamanubhave navabhāsamānatvāttasyānubhavasyādhyastātmaviṣayatvaṃ siddhamkaṇabhakṣākṣacaraṇādikakṣīkṛtasyātmano bhānābhāvādahamanubhavasyādhyastātmaviṣayatvameṣitavyamna tāvadahamanubhavaḥ sarvagatatvagātmanovagamayitumīṣṭeahamihāsmi sadane jānāna iti prādeśikatva grahaṇātna cedaṃ dehasya prādeśikatvaṃ pratibhāsata iti veditavyamahamityullekhāyogātnanu yathā rājñaḥ sarvaprayojanavidhātari bhṛtye mamātmā bhadrasena ityupacārastadvadātmavacana syāhaṃśabdasya deha upacāra iti cet maivaṃ vocaḥupacaritātmabhāvasya dehādeḥ svasamānākṛti śilāputrakādivajjñātṛtvāyogātna ca jñātṛtvamapyupacaritamprayoktuḥ svapratipattiprakāśake prayoge pratipattṛtvopacārānupapatteḥatha dehadharmaḥ prādeśikatvamātmanyupacaryeta tadā dehātmanorbhedena bhavitavyamprasiddhabhede māṇavake siṃhaśabdavatsāṃpratikagauṇatve tirohitabhedena sārṣapādau rase tailaśabdavannirūḍhagauṇatve vā gauṇamukhyayorbhedādhyavasāyasya niyatatvātatha mama śarīramiti bheda bhānasaṃbhavādgauṇatvaṃ manyethāstadayuktamahaṃśabdārthasya dehādibhyo niṣkṛṣyāsādhāraṇadharmavattvena pratibhāsamānatvābhāvātaparathā lokāyatikamataṃ nodayamāsādayetmama śarīramityuktistu rāhoḥ śira itivadaupacārikīmama śarīramiti bruvāṇaonāpi kastvamiti pṛṣṭena vakṣasthalanyastahastena śṛṅgagrāhikayāyamahamiti prativacanasya dīyamānatvena dehātmapratyayasya sakalānubhavasiddhatvāttaduktam  dehātmapratyayo yadvatpramāṇatvena kalpitaḥlaukikaṃ tadvadevedaṃ pramāṇaṃ tvātmaniścayāttathā ca vyāpakasya bhedabhānasya nivṛttervyāpyasya gauṇatvasya nivṛttiriti niravadyamnanvabhijñayā bhedasiddhirmā saṃbhūnnāmapratyabhijñayā tu sohamityevaṃrūpayā tatsiddhiḥ saṃbhaviṣyatīti cennavikalpāsahatvātkimiyaṃ pratyabhijñā pāmarāṇāṃ syātparīkṣakāṇāṃ vānādyaḥdeha vyatiriktātmaikyamavagāhamānāyāḥ pratyabhijñāyā anudayātpratyuta śyāmasya lauhityavatkāraṇaviśeṣādalpasyāpi mahāparimāṇatvamaviruddhamanubhavatāṃ taddeha eva tasyāḥ saṃbhavāccana dvitīyaḥvyavahārasamaye pāmarasāmyānatirekātaparokṣabhramasya parokṣajñānavināśyatvānupapatteścayaduktaṃ bhagavatā bhāṣyakāreṇa pañcādibhiścāviśeṣātbrasūbhā itibhāmatīkārairapyuktaṃ śāstraṃcintakāḥ khalvevaṃ vicārayanti na pratipattāra ititathā cātmagocara syādhyāsātmarūpatvaṃ susthamna cārhatamatānusāreṇāhaṃpratyayaprāmāṇyāyātmano dehaparimāṇatvamaṅgīkaraṇīyamiti sāṃpratammadhyamaparimāṇasya sāvayavatvena dehādivadanityatve kṛtahānākṛtābhyāgamaprasaṅgātathaitaddoṣaparijihīrṣayāvayavasamudāya ātmetyabhyupagamyeta tadā vaktavyamkiṃ pratyekamavayavānāṃ caitanyaṃ sāṃghātasya vānādyaḥbahūnāṃ cetanānāmahamahamikayā pradhānabhāvamanubhavatāmaikamatyābhāvena samasamayaṃ viruddhadikkriyatayāśarīrasyāpi viśaraṇaniṣkriyatvayoranyatarāpātātdvitīyepi saṃghātāpattiḥ kiṃ śarīropādhikī svābhāvikī yādṛcchikī vānādyaḥekasminnavayave chinne cidātmanopyavayavaśchinna ityacetanatvāpātātna dvitīyaḥaneke ṣāmavayavānāmanyonya sāhityaniyamādarśanātna tṛtīyaḥsaṃśleṣavadviśleṣasyāpi yādṛcchikatvena sukhena vasatāmakasmādacetanatvaprasaṅgātna cāṇuparimāṇatvamātmanaḥ śaṅkanīyamsthūlohaṃ dīrghoṃhamiti pratyayānupapatteḥna ca vijñānātmabhāṣiṇāṃ naiṣa doṣaḥviśuddhasāvayavatvābhāvāditi gaṇanīyamyaḥ suṣuptaḥ sohaṃ jāgartīti sthiragocarasyāhamullekhasya kṣaṇabhaṅgivijñānagocaratve atasmistadbuddhirūpa  mithyādhyāsasya tadavasthānāttadanena kṛśohaṃ kṛṣṇohamityādīnāṃ prakhyānānāṃ buddhayā sarūpatākhyānenaupacārikatvaṃ pratyākhyātamtāvyāpakabhedabhānāsaṃbhavasya prāgeva prapañcitatvāttathā ca prayogaḥ  vimataṃ śāstraṃ viṣayaprayojanasahitamāvidyaka bandhanivartakatvātsuptotthitabodhavatyathā svapnāvasthāyāṃ māyāparikalpitayoṣādikṛta bandhanivartakasya suptotthitabodhasya mandiramadhye sukhena śayyāyāmavatiṣṭhamāno deho viṣayaḥtasya suptabodhenāniścayātsvapnamāyāvijṛmbhitānarthanivṛttiḥ prayojanamevaṃ mananādijanyaparokṣa jñānadvāreṇādhyāsikakartṛtvabhoktṛtvādyanarthaniṣedhakasya śāstrasya saccidānandaikarasaṃ pratyagātmabhūtaṃ brahma viṣayaḥtasyāhamanubhavenāniścayātadhyāsanivṛttiḥ prayojanamtathā cāphalatvāditi heturasiddha iti siddhamtaduktam  śrutigamyātmatattvaṃ tu nāhaṃbuddhayāvagamyateapi śve kāmato mohā nātmanyastaviparyayeitoyamasaṃdigdhatvāditi heturapyasiddha iti siddhamyadyapi sarvaḥ prāṇī pratyagātmāstitvaṃ pratyetyahamasmītina hi kaścidapi nāhamasmīti vipratipadyatepratyagātmaiva brahma tattvamasi chā iti sāmānādhikaraṇyāttasmādātmatattvamasaṃdigdhaṃ siddhamtathāpi dharmaṃ prati vipratipannā bahuvidhā iti nyāyena viśeṣapratipattirūpapadyata evatathā hicaitanyaviśiṣṭaṃ dehamātmeti lokāyatā manyanteindriyāṇyātmetyanyeantaḥkaraṇamātmetyaparekṣaṇabhaṅguraṃ saṃtanyamānaṃ vijñānamātmeti bauddhā budhyantedehaparimāṇa ātmeti jainā jināḥ pratijānatekṛrtatvādiviśiṣṭa parameśvarādbhinno jīvātmeti naiyāyikādayo varṇayantidravyabodhasvabhāvamātmetyācāryāḥ paricakṣatebhoktai va ke valaṃ na karteti sāṃkhyāḥ saṃgirantecidrapa ūḥ kartṛtvādirahitaḥ parasmādabhinnaḥ pratyagātmetyaupaniṣadā bhāṣyanteevaṃ prasiddhe dharmiṇi viśeṣato vipratipattau tadviśeṣasaṃśayo yujyatetathā ca saṃdehasaṃbhavājjijñāsyatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ siddhamtaditthaṃ brahmaṇo vicāryatvasaṃbhavena tadvicārātmakaṃ brahmamīmāṃsāśāstramārambhaṇīyamiti yuktamjanmādyasya yataḥbrasū ityādisarvasya śāstrasyaitadvicārāpekṣatvācchāstraprathamādhyāyasaṃgatamidamadhikaraṇamnanvitthaṃbhūte brahmaṇi kiṃ pramāṇaṃ pratyakṣamanumānamāgamo vāna kadācittatra pratyakṣaṃ śramateatīndriyatvātnāpyanumānamvyāptasya liṅgasyābhāvātnāpyāgamaḥyato vāco nivartante tai iti śrutyaivāgamagamyatvaniṣedhātupamānādikamaśakyaśaṅkamniyataviṣayatvāttasmādbrahmaṇi pramāṇaṃ na saṃbhavatīti cet maivaṃ vocaḥpratyakṣādyasaṃbhavepyāgamasya sattvātyato vāco nivartante iti vāgocaratvaniṣedhātkathametaditi cet śrutireva niṣedhati vedāntavedyatvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutireva vidhattena hi vedapratipāditerthenupapanne vaidikānāṃ buddhiḥ khidyateapi tu tadapapādunamārgameva vicārayatitasmādubhayamapi pratipādanīyamviṣātvaniṣedhakāni vākyānivākyajanyavṛttivyaktasphu raṇalakṣaṇaphalāsaṃbhavavivakṣayā pravṛttāniviṣayatvabodhakāni tu vṛttijanyāvaraṇabhaṅgalakṣaṇaphalasaṃbhavavivakṣayātaduktaṃ bhagavadbhiḥ  anādheyaphalatvena śruterbrahma na gocaramprameyaṃ pramitau tu syādātmākārasamarpaṇātna prakāśyaṃ pramāṇena prakāśo brahmaṇaḥ svayamtajjanyāvṛtibhaṅgatvātprameyamiti gīyateiti cananu syādeṣa manoratho yadi siddherthe vedasya prāmāṇyaṃ sidhyetsaṃgatigrahaṇāyattatvātprāmāṇya niścayasyasaṃgatigrahaṇasya ca vṛddhavyavahārāyattatvātvṛddhavyavahārasya ca loke kāryaikaniyatatvātna hyasti saṃbhavaḥ śabdānāṃ kāryerthe saṃgatigrahaḥ siddhārthābhidhāyakatvaṃ tatra vā prāmāṇyamitina hi turaṅgatve gṛhītasaṃgatikaṃ turaṅgapadaṃ gotvamācaṣṭe tatra vā prāmāṇyaṃ bhajatetasmātkāryagṛhītasaṃgatikānāṃ śabdānāṃ kārya eva prāmāṇyamnanu mukhavikāsādiliṅgāddharṣahetuṃ prasiddhārthamanumāya yatra śabdasya saṃgatigraho yathā putraste jāta ityādiṣu tatrāvaśyaṃ kāryamantareṇaiva śabdasya siddherthe prāmāṇyamāśrīyata iti cennaputrajanmavadeva priyāsukhaprasavāderanekasya harṣahetorupasthīyamānatvena pariśeṣāvadhāraṇānupapatteḥputraste jāta ityādiṣu siddhārthapareṣu prayogeṣu dvāraṃ dvāramityādivatkāryādhyāhāreṇa prayogopapatteścaśāstratvaprasiddhayā ca na vedāntānāṃ siddhārthaparatvampravṛttinivṛttiparāṇāmeva vākyānāṃ śāstratvaprasiddheḥtaduktaṃ bhaṭṭācāryaiḥ  pravṛttirvā nivṛttirvā nityena kṛtake na vāpuṃsāṃ yenopadiśyeta tacchāstramabhidhīyatena caiteṣāṃ svarūpaparatve prayojanamastiśrutavedāntārthasyāpi puṃsaḥ sāṃsārikadharmāṇāmanivṛtteḥtasmādvedāntānāmapyātmā jñātavya iti samāmnātena vidhinaikavākyatāmāśritya kāryaparataivāśraya ṇīyeti siddhamtataśca ke valasiddharūpe brahmaṇi vedāntānāṃ prāmāṇyaṃ na sidhyatīti cetatra pratividhīyate na tāvatsiddhe vyutpattyasiddhiḥprāgunnītayā nītyā putraste jāta iti vākyātsiddhaparādapi vyutpattisiddheḥna ca pariśeṣāvadhāraṇānupapattiḥpriyāsukhaprasavāderapi saṃbhavāditi bhaṇitavyamputrapadāṅkitapaṭapradarśanavatpriyāsukhaprasavādi sūcakābhāvātputrajanmaiva tatsūcakamiti cet prathamapratītaputrajanmaparityāge kāraṇābhāvātputrajananasyaivādhikānanda hetutvāccaputrotpattivipattibhyāṃ nāparaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥiti vidyamānatvāttathā cākathaccitsukhācāryaḥ  dṛṣṭacaitrasutotpattestatpadāṅkitavāsasāvārtāhāreṇa yātasya pariśeṣaviniściteḥcitsupṛ itiyaduktaṃ siddhārthapareṣu kāryādhyāhāra iti tadayuktammukhyārthaviṣayatayā siddhepi prayogasiddhāvadhyāhārānupapatteḥyaduktaṃ śāstratvaprasiddhayā ca na svarūpaparatvamiti tadapyayuktamhitaśāsanādapi śāstratvopapatteḥna ca prayojanābhāvaḥśrutamatavedāntadrajanyādvitīyā tmavijñānābhyāsena vidyodaye saṃsāranidānāvidyānivṛttyupalakṣitabrahmātmatālakṣaṇaparamapuruṣārthasiddheḥna cātra vidhiḥ saṃbhavativikalpāsahatvāttathā hikiṃ śābdajñānaṃ vidheyaṃ kiṃ vā bhāvanātmakamāhosvitsākṣātkārarūpamnādyaḥviditapadārthasaṃgatikasyādhītaśabdanyāya tattvasyāntareṇapi vidhiṃ śabdādevopapatteḥnāpi dvitīyaḥbhāvanāyā jñānaprakarṣahetu bhāvasyānvayavyatirekasiddhatayā prāptatvenāvidheyatvātaprāptaprāpakasyaiva vidhitvāṅgīkārāttṛtīye sākṣātkāraḥ kiṃ brahmasvarūpaḥ kiṃ vāntaḥkaraṇapariṇāmabhedaḥnādyaḥtasya nityatvenāvidheyatvātnāpi dvitīyaḥānandasākṣātkārarūpatayā phalatvenāvidheyatvāttasmājjñātavya ityādīnāmavidhāyakatvādarhe kṛtyatṛcaśca pāsū  iti kṛtyapratyayānamarhārthe vidhānādarhārthataiva vyākhyeyātathā ca sarveṣāṃvedāntavākyānāmupakramopa saṃhāradiṣaḍvidhatātparyoṃpetatvānnityaśuddhabuddhamuktasvabhāvabrahmātmaparatvamāstheyamniṣpradeśe paramāṇau pradeśavṛttitvenābhimatasya saṃyogasya darupapādunatayā tannibandhanasya dvaṇukasyāsiddhau dyaṇukādikrameṇārambhavādasaṃbhavādacetanāyāḥ prakṛtermahadādirūpeṇa pariṇāmavādā saṃbhavācca khyātibādhānyathānupapattyānirvacanīyaḥ prapañcaścidvivarta iti siddhamsvarūpāparityāgena rūpāntarāpattirvivarta iti satyamithyākhyāvabhāsa itiavabhāsodhyāsa iti paryāyaḥsa cādhyāso dvividhaḥ arthādhyāso jñānādhyāsaścetitaduktam  pramāṇadoṣasaṃskārajanmānyasya parātmatātaddhīścādhyāsa iti hi dvayamiṣṭaṃ manīṣibhiḥpunarapi dvividhodhyāsaḥnirupādhikasopādhikabhedāttadapyuktam  doṣeṇa karmaṇā vāpi kṣobhitājñānasaṃbhavaḥtattvavidyāvirodhī ca bhramoyaṃ nirupādhikaḥupādhisaṃnidhiprāptakṣobhāvidyāvijṛmbhitamupādhyapagamāpohyamāhuḥ sopādhikaṃ bhramamtatra svarūpeṇa kalpitāhamādyadhyāso nirūpādhikaḥtadapyuktam  nīlimeva viyatyeṣā bhrāntyā brahmaṇi saṃsṛtiḥghaṭavyomeva bhoktāyaṃ bhrānto bhedena sa svataḥata eva bhāṣyakāraḥ śuktikā rajatavadavabhāsata ekaścandraḥ sa dvitīyavaditi nidarśanadvayamudājahāraśiṣṭaṃ śāstra eva spaṣṭamiti vistarabhiyoparamyateevaṃ ca dṛgdṛśyau dvāveva padārthāviti vedāntināṃ siddhānta iti sarvamavadātamatra prabhākaraḥ śuktikā rajatavadavabhāsata iti dṛṣṭānto neṣṭaḥrajatapratyayasya śuktikālambanatvānupapatteḥtathā hi idaṃ rajatamiti pratītau śukte rālambanatvaṃ purodeśasattāmātreṇā valambyate kāraṇatvena bhāsamānatvena vānādyaḥpurovartināṃ loṣṭādīnāmapyālambanatvaprasaṅgātatha kaladhautabodhakaraṇasaṃskārodbodhakāraṇatvena taddvārā rajatajñānakāraṇatvādālambanatvaṃ manyasetadapi na saṃgacchatecakṣurādīnāmapi kāraṇatvena viṣayatvāpātātatha bhāsamānatayā viṣayatvamiṣyate tadapyaśliṣṭamrajatanirbhāsasya śuktikālambanatvānupapatteḥyasminvijñāne yadavabhāsate tattadālambanamatra ca kaladhautānubhavaḥ śaktikālambanatvakalpanāyāṃ virudhyatetathā cācakathannayāyavīthyāṃ śālikanāthaḥ atra brūmo ya evārthoṃ yasyāṃ saṃvidi bhāsatevedyaḥ sa eva nānyaddhi vedyāvedyatvalakṣaṇamidaṃ rajatamityatra rajataṃ tvavabhāsatetadeva tena vedyaṃ syānna tu śuktiravedanāttenānyasyānyathā bhāsaḥ pratītyaiva parāhataḥanyasminbhāsamāne hi na paraṃ bhāsate yataḥprakapa itikiṃ ca mithyājñānotpattau sāmagrī na samastikiṃ ke valānīndriyādīni kāraṇāni doṣadūṣitāni vānādyaḥteṣāṃ samīcīnajñāna jananasāmarthyoṃpalambhātanyathā samīcīnaṃ rajatajñānaṃ kadācidadayamāsāduyet na dvitīyaḥdoṣāṇāmautsargikakāryaprasava śaktipratibandhamātraprabhāvatvātna hi duṣṭaṃ ku ṭajabījaṃ vaṭāṅku raṃ janayitumīṣṭena vā tailakaluṣitaṃ śālibījamaśālyaṅku ra jananāyālamkiṃ tu svakāryaṃ na karotinanu dāvadahanadagdhasya vetrabījasya kadalīkāṇḍajanakatvaṃ dṛṣṭamiti cet tanna sthānedagdhasyāvetrabījatvena doṣāṇāṃ viparītakāryakāritvaṃ pratyanudāharaṇātna ca bhasmakadoṣadūṣitasya kaukṣeyasyāśuśukṣaṇerbahvannapacana sāmarthyaṃ dṛṣṭamityeṣṭavyamaśitapītādyāhārapariṇatau jāṭharasya jātavedasaḥ śaktatvāttaduktam  ayathārthasya bodhasya notpattāvasti kāraṇamdoṣāścenna hi doṣāṇāṃ kāryaśaktivighātatābhasmakādiṣu kāryasya vighātādeva doṣatāagnerhi rasaniṣpattiḥ kāryaṃ jaṭharavartinaḥpraka pa  itiapi cāsatyapyarthe jñānaprādurbhāvābhyupagame samīcīnasthalepi jñānānāṃ svagocaravyabhicāraśaṅkā ṅku rasaṃbhavena niraṅku śo vyavahāro lupyatetadāha  yadi cārthaṃ parityajya kācidbaddhi uḥ prakāśatevyabhicāravati svārthe kathaṃ viśvāsakāraṇampraka pa  itinanu rajatagocaraikaviśiṣṭajñānānaṅgīkāre viśiṣṭavyavahāro na sidhyetatastatsiddhayepi viparyayoṅgīkārya iti cennaidaṃ rajatamiti grahaṇasmaraṇābhidhasya bodhadvayasya vyavahārakāratvāṅgīkārātyadyevamidaṃ śuktikāśakalaṃ tadrajatamityatopi viśiṣṭavyavahāraḥ syādititannatatredamiti purovartidravyamātragrahaṇasya doṣadūṣitacakṣurjanyatvenānākalita  śuktitvādiviśeṣitasya sāmānyamātragrahaṇarūpatvādrajatamiti jñānasyāsaṃnihitaviṣayasya saṃprayoga liṅgādyaprasūtatayā sadṛśāvabodhitasaṃskāramātraprabhavatvena pariśeṣaprāptasmṛtibhāvasya doṣahetukatayā gṛhītatattāṃśapramoṣādgrahaṇamātratvopapatteḥtadapyuktam  nanvatra rajatābhāsaḥ kathameṣa ghaṭiṣyateucyate śuktiśakalaṃ gṛhītaṃ bhedavarjitamśuktikāyā viśeṣā ye rajatādbhedahetavaḥte na jñātā abhibhavājjñātā sāmānyarūpatāanantaraṃ ca rajatasmṛtirjātā tayāpi camanodoṣāttadityaṃśaparāmarśavivarjitamrajataṃ viṣayīkṛtya naiva śukte rvivecitamsmṛtyāto rajatābhāsa upapanno bhavaṣyitipraka pa  na hyasaṃnihitaṃ tāvatpratyakṣaṃ rajataṃ bhavetliṅgādyabhāvāccānyasya pramāṇasya na gocaraḥpariśeṣātsmṛtiriti niścayo jāyate punaḥpraka pa  nanu kimidamekai kaṃ vyavahārakāraṇamuta saṃbhūyana prathamaḥdeśabhedena pravṛttiprasaṅgātna caramaḥprayatnāyaugapadyājjñānā yogapadyāt  vaisū ityādinā jñānayaugapadyaniṣedhātato jñānadvayaṃ heturityayuktaṃ vaca iti cet maivaṃ vocaḥavinaśyatoḥ sahāvasthānaniṣedhepi vinaśyadavinaśyatoḥ sahāvasthānasyāniṣiddhatvena nirantarotpannayostadupapatteḥnanu rajatajñānādrajatārthī rajate pravartatāṃ nāmapaurastye vastuni kathaṃ pravṛttiḥ syāditi cennasvarūpato viṣayataścāgṛhītabhedayorgrahaṇa smaraṇayoḥ saṃnihitarajatagocarajñānasārūpyeṇa vastutaḥ parasparaṃ vibhinnayorapyabhedocitasāmānādhikaraṇya vyapadeśahetutvopapatteḥgrahaṇasmaraṇayoḥ saṃnihitarajatajñānasārūpyaṃ kathamyathā caitattathā niśamyatāmsaṃnihitarajatagocaraṃ hi vijñānamidamaṃśarajatāṃśayorasaṃsarga nāvagāhatetayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭatvenāsaṃsargasyaivābhāvātnāpi svagataṃ bhedamekajñānatvātevaṃ grahaṇasmaraṇe api doṣavaśādvidyamānamapīdamaṃśarajatāṃśayorasaṃsarga bhedaṃ nāvagāhata itibhedāgrahaṇameva sārūpyamtaduktaṃ gurumatānusāribhiḥ  grahaṇasmaraṇe ceme vivekānavabhāsinīsamyagrajatabodhācca bhinne yadyapi tattvataḥtathāpi bhinne nābhāte bhedāgrahasamatvataḥsamyagrajatabodhastu samakṣaikārthagocaraḥtato bhinne abuddhā ca grahaṇasmaraṇe imesamānenaiva rūpeṇa ke valaṃ manyate janaḥaparokṣāvabhāsena samānārthagraheṇa caavailakṣaṇyasāṃvīttiriti tāvatsamarthitāvyavahāropi tattulyastata eva pravartateprakapa evamagṛhītavivekamāpannasaṃnihitarūpyajñānasārūpyaṃ grahaṇasmaraṇadvayamayathāvyavahāraheturiti siddhamyadyevamayathāvyavahāro grahaṇa smaraṇajanyastarhi pītaḥ śaṅkha ityādau sa na siddhastatra tayorabhāvāditi cennaagṛhītavivekayoḥ prāptasamīcīnasaṃsargajñānasārupyatve grahaṇayoreva vyavahārasaṃpādakatvopapatteḥnayanaraśmivartinaḥ pittadravyasya pītimādoṣa vaśāddravyarahito gṛhyateśaṅkhopyakalitaśuklaguṇaḥ svarūpato gṛhyatetadanayorguṇaguṇinoḥ saṃsargayogyayorasaṃsargāgraha sārūpyātpītatapanīyapiṇḍapratyayāvailakṣaṇyābdavahāra upapadyateyathoktam  pītaśaṅkhāvabodhe hi pittāsyendriyavartinaḥpītimā gṛhyate dravyarahito doṣatastathāśaṅkhasyendriyadoṣeṇa śuklimā na ca gṛhyateke valaṃ dravyamātraṃ tu prathate rūpavarjitamguṇe dravyavyapekṣe ca dravye ca guṇakāṅkṣiṇibhāsamāne tayorbuddhirasaṃbandhaṃ na budhyatesatyapītāvabhāsena same bhāte matī imevyavahāropi tattulyaṃ evamatrāpi yujyatepraka pa  itinanvidaṃ rajatamiti bhrāntijñānānabhyupagame rajataprasakte rasattvānnedaṃ rajatamiti niṣedhaḥ kathaṃ kaladhautābhāvaṃ bodhayatīti cet naiṣa doṣaḥbhedāgrahaprasañjitasya śuktau rajatavyavahārasya niṣedhasvīkāreṇa kalpanā lāghavasadbhāvāttaduktaṃ pañcikāprakaraṇe  mithyābhāvopi tattulyavyavahārapravartanātrajatavyavahārāṃśe visaṃvādayato narātbādhaka pratyayasyāpi bādhakatvamato matamprasajyamānarajatavyavahārānavāraṇātpraka pa  ititadanena prācīnayorjñānayoḥ satyatve kathaṃ bhramatvaprasiddhiriti śaṅkā parākṛtāayathāvyavahāra pravartakatvena tadupapatteḥkiṃ ca nedaṃ rajatamiti bādhakāvabodho nābhāvamavagāhatebhāvavyatireke ṇābhāvasya durgrahaṇatvātyadyevamaṅga nāstīti pratyayasya kimālambanamaparathā māhābhānikapakṣānupraveśa iti cet maivaṃ bhāṣiṣṭhāḥabhāvasya dhārmipratiyoginirūpaṇādhīnanirupyatvevāvaśyābhyupagamanīye dṛśye pratiyogi nyadṛśye vā smaryamāṇedhikaraṇamātrabuddherevanāstīti vyavahāropapattāvatiriktā bhāvakalpanāyāṃ pramāṇābhāvāttaduktamamṛtakalāyām  atrocyate dvayī saṃvidvastuno bhūtalādinaḥekā saṃsṛṣṭaviṣayā tanmātraviṣayā parātanmātraviṣayā vāpi dvayī sātha nigadyatepratiyoginyadṛśye ca dṛśye ca pratiyoginitatra tanmātradhīryeyaṃ smṛte ca pratiyoginināstitvaṃ saiva bhūbhāge ghaṭādipratiyoginaḥpraka pa  itiata eva ca prābhākaramatānusāribhiḥ pramāṇapārāyaṇe pratyakṣādīnipañcaiva pramāṇāni prapañcitāninanvevamabhāvasyābhāve nakārasya vaiyarthyamāpadyetaanuśāsanavirodhaścāpatediti cet  tadetadvārtamekonapañcāśadvarṇānāṃ madhye kasyāpi varṇasyābhāvārthatvādarśanena varṇasya sato nakārasya tadarthatvānupapatteḥna caivamanuśāsanavirodhaḥtadanyatadabhāvatadviruddheṣvartheṣvanuśāsanasyaivamarthaḥ syāttathā hi cetanānāṃ madhye kaścana kasyacicchatruḥ kaścana kasyācinmitraṃ kaścana kasya cidudāsīnastathaivā cetanānāmapitadanyapadena tadudāsīno nakārārthaḥviruddhapadena śatrurnakārārthaḥtadabhāvapadena mitraṃ nakārārthaḥtathā cābrāhmaṇapada evaitattrayaṃ pratīyate śūdra ityudāsīno yavana iti śatruḥ kṣatriya iti mitramevaṃ sarvatra nañprayogasthale draṣṭavyamiti na kaścidabhāvo bhāvavyatiriktaḥ saṃbhavatitasmāduktayā rītyā bhramaprasiddhayā vivādādhyāsitāḥ pratyayā yathārthāḥ pratyayatvāddaṇḍīti pratyayavaditi siddhamtadapare na kṣamanteiha khalu nikhilaprekṣāvānsamīhitatatsādhanayoranyatarapravedane pravartatena ca rajatamarthayamānasya śuktikāśakalajñānaṃ tadrūpamanu bhāvayituṃ prabhavatiśuktikāśakalasya samīhitatatsādhanayoranyatarabhāvābhāvātnāpi rajatasmaraṇaṃ purovartini pravṛttikāraṇamtasyānubhavapārantryatayānubhavadeśa eva pravartakatvātnāpi bhedāgraho vyavahārakāraṇamgrahaṇanibandhatvāccetanevyavahārasyananu na vayamekai kasya kāraṇatvaṃ brūmahe yenaivamupālabhyemahikiṃ tvagṛhītavivekasya jñānadvayasya prāptasamīcīnapuraḥsthitarajatajñānasārūpyasyetyanukto pālambhoyamiti cet tadapyayuktamvikalpāsahatvāttathā hi samīcīnarajatāvabhāsasārūpyaṃ bhāsamānaṃ pravartakaṃ sattāmātreṇa vāādye vikalpe bhedāgrahāparaparyāyasya sārūpyasya samīcīnasaṃnibhe ime jñāne iti viśeṣākāreṇa gṛhyamāṇasya pravṛttikāraṇatvaṃ kiṃ vānayoreva svarūpato viṣayataśca mitho bhedāgraho vidyata iti sāmānyākāreṇa gṛhyamāṇasya sārūpyasyanādyaḥsamīcīnajñānavattatsaṃnibhajñānasya taducitavyavahārapravartakatvānupapatteḥna khalu gosaṃnibho gavaya ityavabhāso gavārthinaṃ samāna iti vācyamrajatatvasya hetoḥ pakṣadharmatvābhāvātna ca pakṣadharmatāyā abhāvepi vyāptibalādvamakatvaṃ śaṅkayamvyāptipakṣa dharmatāvalliṅgasyaiva gamakatvāṅgīkārāttadāhuḥ śabarasvāminaḥ tadviṣayatvamavagamayati vilumpati jñānābhāvakoṭayantaramiti kva saṃdehāvakāśaḥtadevaṃ lakṣaṇāhetvabhāvenubhavābhāvopyātmani na pratyakṣeṇa gṛhyata iti pariśeṣāduktalakṣaṇāvidyaivājña iti pratibhāsasya viṣaya iti sthitamastu vā jñānābhāvapratibhāsaḥayamabhāvaśca pratiyogī yatra niṣidhyate na tatastattvāntaramanyadadhikaraṇabhāvātmā bhūdanya bhāvatvamanyābhāvatvaṃ tu syātnanu tadapi viruddhamsatyaṃ sati bhedesa ca pramāṇāttacca sati pratiyogyabhāvādhikaraṇatastattvāntarenanu ghaṭavati bhūtale ghaṭābhāvamitivyavahṛtī syātāmiti cet mā bhūtāmete pratiyoginā kalpanāgauramevatathā hi tattvāntaratvaṃ tāvedakaṃ kalpyamtasyāparokṣatvāyendriyasaṃnikarṣaḥ kalpyaḥsa ca saṃyogādirna bhavatīti saṃyuktaviśeṣaṇatvādiḥ kalpya ityato varamuktalakṣaṇasyādhikaraṇasya vyavahāraviṣayeṅgīkāraḥsati caivaṃ jñānābhāvenāpi pratiyogismṛtau satyāmanubhūyamānamadhikaraṇaṃ jñātaivasa ca na ke valamantaḥkaraṇamjaḍatvātnāpi ke vala ātmaivaapariṇāmitvādaguṇatvāccaata ubhayorabhedādhyāsaḥātmādhyāsaścoktalakṣaṇā vidyātmetyāyātamavidyāyāmevāhamajña iti pratibhāsaḥ pramāṇamitianumānaṃ ca  vivādapadaṃ pramāṇajñānaṃ svaprāgabhāvavyatiriktasvaviṣayāvaraṇasvanivartyasvadeśa gatavastvantarapūrvaka prakāśitārthaprakāśakatvātandhakāre prathamotpannapradīpaprabhāvaditivastupūrvakamityukta ātmavastu pūrvakatvenārthāntaratātadarthaṃ vastvantaretitathāpi viṣayabhūte vastvantarerthāntaratātadarthaṃ svadeśagatetiadṛṣṭādikaṃ pratyādeṣṭuṃ svanivartyetiuttarajñānanivartyaṃ prathamajñānaṃ nivartayituṃ svaviṣayāvaraṇetiprāgabhāvaṃ pratikṣeptuṃ svaprāgabhāvavyatirikte tisvaprāgabhāvavyatiriktapūrvakamityukte viṣayeṇārthāntaratātadarthaṃ viṣayāvaraṇetitādṛśamandhakāraṃ vyāseddhaṃu svanivartyetiviṣayagatāmajñātatāṃ nirākartṛṃ svadeśagatetimithyājñānamapohituṃ vastvantaretidhārāvāhikavijñāne vyabhicāraṃ vyāseddhumaprakāśitetimadhyavartipradīpaprabhāyāṃ sādhyasādhanavaidhuryapratirodhāya prathamotpannaviśeṣaṇamsaurālokavyāptadeśasthapradīpaprabhāpratikṣepāyā ndhakāretina ca jñānasādhake pramāṇe vyabhicāraḥ śaṅkanīyaḥvipratipannaṃ pratyasattvanivṛttimātrasya pramāṇakṛtyatvāttaduktaṃ devatādhikaraṇe kalpatarukārairanumānādi bhirasattvanivṛttiḥ kriyata itinanu sādhanavikalo dṛṣṭānta iti cennaprakāśaśabdena tamovirodhyākārasya vivakṣitatvāttaduktaṃ vivaraṇavivaraṇe sahajasarvajñaviṣṇubhaṭṭopādhyāyaiḥ  na cātra pakṣadṛṣṭāntayorekaprakāśarūpānanvayaḥ śaṅkanīyaḥtamovirodhyākāro hi prakāśaśabdavācyaḥtenākāreṇaikyamubhayatrāstītinarendragiriśrīcaraṇaustvitthamuktamaaprakāśitaprakāśavyavahārahetutvaṃ hetvarthaḥtasya cobhayatrānugatatvānnāsiddhayādiritiśruteścabhūyaścānte viśvamāyānivṛttiḥ śve ityādikā śrutiḥtaratyavidyāṃ vitatāṃ hṛdi yasminniveśiteyogī māyāmameyāya tasmai vidyātmane namaḥiti caetenaitatpratyuktaṃ yaduktaṃ bhāskareṇa kṣapaṇakacaraṇaṃ pramāṇaśaraṇe bhedābhedavādināṃ bhāvarūpajñānaṃ nāsti kiṃ tu jñānābhāva ititathā ca bhāskarapraṇītaśārīrakamīmāṃsābhāṣyagranthaḥyadeva pararūpādarśanaṃ saivāvidyeti bhāvarūpājñānānabhyupagame jīveśvarādivibhāgā nupapatteḥna ca bhāvikaḥ paramātmanoṃśo jīva iti vācyamniṣkalaṃ niṣkriyaṃ śāntaṃ niravadyaṃ nirañjanam ityādiśrutivirodhātke cana śāktāḥ  śaktiṃ māyāśabdārthabhūtāṃ jagatkāraṇatvenāṅgīkṛtāṃ satyāmabhyupetya mātuliṅgagadākheṭavidhāriṇī mahālakṣmīstasyāḥ prathamāvatāra iti varṇayantisā ca kālarātriḥ sarasvatīti dve śaktī utpādya brāhmaṇaṃ puruṣaṃ śriyaṃ ca striyamutpādayāmāsasvayaṃ mithunaṃ janayitvā svasute apyāhaahamiva yuvāmapi mithunamutpādayatamititataḥ kālarātrirmahādevaṃ puruṣaṃ svarāṃ striyaṃ ca janayāmāsasarasvatī ca viṣṇuṃ puruṣaṃ gaurīṃ ca striyamudapādayattataścādirvivāhamakarodakārayaccaevaṃ brahmaṇe svarāṃ viṣṇave śriyaṃ śivāya gaurīṃ dattvā śaktiyuktānāṃ teṣāṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārākhyāni karmāṇi pratyapādayadititadetanmataṃ śrutyādimūlapramāṇavidhuratayā svotprekṣāmātraparikalpitamiti svarūpavyākriyaiva nirākriyetyupekṣaṇīyamtataścānirvacanīyānādya vidyālasitaḥ pratyagātmani pratīyamānaḥ pramātṛtvādiprapañca ityalamatiprasaṅgenananu kimarthaṃ pramātṛtvādīnāmāvidyakatvaṃ nigadyatebrahmajñānena nivartanāya jīvasya brahmabhāvāya vāna prathamaḥśāstraprāmāṇyādeva satyasyāpi jñānena nivṛtterūpapatteḥupalambhāccatathāhi  setuṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyata brahmahā brahmahatyayāityādinā pāpaṃ sanīstrasyateviṣayadoṣadarśanena rāgo dandahyatetārkṣyadhyānena viṣaṃ śamyateevaṃ katṛtvādibandhaḥ pāramārthikopi tattvajñānena nivartyetana caramaḥaupādhikasya jīvabhāvasyopādhinivṛttyā nivṛttau brahmabhāvasaṃbhavāttasmādvandhasyāvidyakatva vācoyuktiḥ sāvadyeti cet naitadanavadyamsatyasyātmavajjñānanivartyatvānupapatteḥbandhasya mithyātvamantareṇa śāstraprāmāṇyādapi tadasiddheścaśāstramapilokāvagatasāmarthyaḥ śabdo vedepi bodhakaḥiti nyāyena lokāvalokitāṃ padaśaktiṃ padārthayogyatāṃ corarīkṛtya pracaratītiaparathā ādityo yūpaḥ taibrā yajamānaḥ prastaraḥ taisaṃ iyādivākyastomasya yathāśruterthe prāmāṇyāpatteḥvaidikyāḥ kriyāyāḥ samakṣakṣayitayā pāratrikaphalakaraṇatvānyathānupapattyā apūrvāṅgīkaraṇānupapattiścaloke ca śuktivyaktitattvābhivyaktāvapanīyamānasyāropitasya mithyātva dṛṣṭau taddṛṣṭāntāvaṣṭambhenātmatattvasākṣātkāravidyāpanodyasyāvidyakasya bandhasya mithyātvānumāna saṃbhavātvimataṃ mithyā adhiṣṭhānattvajñānanivartyatvācchu ktikārūpyavaditina ca vimataṃ satyaṃ bhāsamānatvāditi pratiprayoge samānabalatayā bādhapratirodhaḥpratirodhabhiyānyatara doṣatvasaṃbhavāditi vaditavyammarumarīcikodakādau savyabhicārātabādhitatvena viśeṣaṇānna doṣa iti cet maivaṃ bhāṣiṣṭhāḥviśeṣaṇāsiddheḥtatredaṃ bhavānpṛṣṭo vyācaṣṭāmkatipayapuruṣa katipayakālābādhitatvaṃ hetuviśeṣaṇaṃ kriyate sarvathā bādhavaidhuryaṃ vāna prathamaḥyatnenānumitopyarthaḥ ku śalairanumātṛbhiḥabhiyuktatarairanyairanyathaivopapādyatevākyapa iti nyāyena tricaturapratipattṛpratipāditasyāpi pratipattrantareṇa prakārāntaramurarīkṛtya pratipādanātnāpi caramaḥsarvadhā bādhabaidhuryasyāsarvajñadurjñeyatvātyadyevaṃ hanta tarhi jñānātmanopi satyatvaṃ nāvagamyata iti cet maivaṃ maṃsthāḥtatsatyaṃ sa ātmā chā ityāgamasaṃvādagateḥna ca prapañcepyayaṃ nyāya iti mantavyamtādṛśasyāgamasyānupalambhātpratyutādvitīyatvaṃ śrāvayantyāḥ śruteḥ prapañcamithyātva eva pakṣapātātnanu kalpanāmātraśarīrasya pakṣasapakṣavipakṣādeḥ sarvasulabhatvena jayaparājayavyavasthāyā kathaṃ kathā prathetakātra kathaṃtāevaṃ tricaturajñānajanmano nādhikā matiḥślovā sūtre iti nyāyena tricaturakakṣyāviśrāntasya tattadābhāsalakṣaṇānāliṅgitasya dūṣaṇabhūṣaṇādestatra kathāṅgatvā ṅgīkārātata evoktaṃ khaṇḍanakāreṇavyāvahārikīṃ pramāṇasattāmādāya vicārārambhaḥ khapṛ itina ca bhedagrāhibhiḥ pramāṇairadvaitaśruterjaghanyatetiśaṅkayambrahmaṇi pāramārthikasatyatvena tadāvedikāyāstattvāvedana lakṣaṇaprāmāṇyāyāḥ śrutervyāvahārikapramāṇabhāvānāṃ pratyakṣādīnāṃ ca vibhinnaviṣayatayā parasparaṃ bādhyabādhakabhāvāsaṃbhavāttadapyuktaṃ tenaiva  tadadvaitaśrutestāvadvādhaḥ pratyakṣataḥ kṣataḥnānumānādi taṃ kartuṃ tavāpi kṣamate matekha dhīdhanā bādhanāyāsyāstadā prajñāṃ prayacchathakṣeptuṃ cintāmaṇiṃ pāṇilabdhamabdhau yadīcchathakha tasmāttattvajñānena nivartanāyāsya bandhasyājñānakalpitatvamaṅgīkartavyamyata uktaṃ yato jñānamajñānasya nivartakamitiyaduktaṃ satyasyāpi duritasya setudarśanena nivṛttirūpalabhyata kvaciddarśanakriyāyā api vidhānaṃ darīdṛśyata iti cet maivaṃ vocaḥtatrāpyanayai vānupapattyāgnicidādyarghaparicaryādāveva tātparyāvadhāraṇātyaccoktaṃ viṣayadoṣadarśanādrāgo dandahyata ititatra viṣayadoṣadarśanena virodhabhūtānabhiratisaṃjñakavairāgyaikaprādurbhāvādrāganivṛttau tadadarśana mātramiti na vyabhicāraḥyadapi tārkṣyadhyānādinā viṣādi satyaṃ vinaśyatītitanna śliṣyatetatrāpi mantraprayogādikriyāyā eva viṣādyapanodakatvātdhyānasya pramātvābhāvāccayadavādyaupādhikasya jīvabhāvasyopādhikanivṛtyā nivṛttau brahmabhāvopapatterna tadarthamarthavaitathya kathanamititadapi kāśaku vyasanitayāyadi vastutaḥ sarvoṃpadravarahitamātmatattvaṃ tarhi kathaṃkāraṃ dehādirūpaṃ kārāgāraṃ kāraṃkāraṃ punaḥpunastatra praviśatitadatiphalguavidyāyā anāditvena dattottaratvātato nivṛttyupāya evānveṣaṇīyaḥ prekṣāvatāna tu vismayaḥ kartavyaḥtataśca tattvamasyādividyayā tadavidyānivṛttau niratiśayānandātmalābharūpaparamapuruṣārthaḥ setsyatitathā cāpastambasmṛtiḥ  ātmalābhānna paraṃ vidyata itinanvasau nityalabdhaḥna hi svayameva svasyālabdho bhavatisatyamkiṃ tvanādimāyāsaṃbandhātkṣīrodaka vatsamudācāravṛttitāṃ na labhatetathā ca yathā śabarādibhirbālyā tsvasutaiḥ saha vardhito rājaputrastajjātīyamātmānamavagacchanbandhubhirya evaṃbhūto rājā sa tvamasīti bodhite svarūpe labdhasvarūpa iva bhavati tathā veśyāsthānīyayānādyavidyayā svabhāvāntaraṃ nīta ātmā mātṛsthānīyayā tattvamasītyādikayā śrutyā svabhāvaṃ nīyate etadāhustraividyavṛddhāḥ  nīcānāṃ vasato tadīyatanayai sārdhaṃ ciraṃ vardhitastajjātīyamavaiti rājatanayaḥ svātmānamapyañjasāsaṃvāde mahadādibhiḥ saha vasaṃstadvadbhavetpuruṣaḥ svātmānaṃ sukhaduḥkhajālakalitaṃ mithyaiva dhiṅmanyatedātā bhogaparaḥ samagravibhavo yaḥ śāsitā duṣkṛtām rājā sa tvamasīti rakṣitṛmukhācchrutvā yathāvatsa turājībhūya jayārthameva yatate tadvatpumānbodhitaḥ śrutyā tattvamasītyapāsya duritaṃ brahmaiva saṃpadyateetenaitatpratyuktaṃ yaduktaṃ paraiḥ kiṃ dvayostādātmyamekasya vānādyaḥadvaitabhaṅgaprasaṅgātna dvitīyaḥasaṃbhavādititannaavidyāparikalpitabhedanivṛttiparatvena tattvamasyāditādātmya vādaprāmāṇyopapatteḥtau ca paryanuyogaparihārāvagrāhiṣātāṃ manīṣibhiḥna dvayorasti tādātmyaṃ na caikasyādvayatvataḥapramāṇyaṃ śruterevaṃ nāropadhvaṃsamātrataḥtataśca tattvamasīti tattvaṃpadārthaśravaṇamananabhāvanābalabhuvā sākṣātkāreṇānādyavidyānivṛttau saccidānandaikarasavrahmāvirbhāvaḥ saṃpatsyata iti brahmaṇo jijñāsyatvaṃ prathamasūtroktaṃ yuktamajñātaṃ viṣayo brahma jñātaṃ tacca prayojanammumukṣuradhikārī syātsaṃbandhaḥ śaktitaḥ śruteḥjanmādyasya yataḥ brasū iti dvitīyasūtre brahma svarūpalakṣaṇataṭasthalakṣaṇābhyāṃ nyarūpitatra svarūpāntargatatve sati vyāvartakaṃ svarūpalakṣaṇaṃ satyaṃ jñānamanantaṃ brahma tai ityādi vedāntaiḥ pratipāditamtasya satyajñānādyātmakasvarūpāntargatatve sati vyāvartakatvāttaṭasthalakṣaṇaṃ yato vā imānitai ityādīni vākyāni nirūpayanti jagajjanmādi kāraṇatvenataduktaṃ vivaraṇe  jagajjanmasthitidhvaṃsā yataḥ sidhyanti kāraṇāttatsvarūpataṭasthābhyāṃ lakṣaṇābhyāṃ pradarśyateśāstrayonitvāt  brasū  iti tṛtīyasūtre prathamavarṇake na ṣaṣṭhīsamāsamāśritya sarvajñatvaṃ pratyapādidvitīyavarṇake na bahubrīhi samāsamabhyupagamya brahmaṇo vedāṃntapramāṇakatvaṃ pratyajñāyitattu samanvayāt  brasū iti caturthe sūtre prathamavarṇake na vedāntānāṃ brahmaṇi tātparyaṃ pratyapādidvitīyavarṇake na vedāntānāṃ pratipattividhiśeṣatayā brahmaprātipādakatvaṃ pratyakṣepidiṅmātramatra pradarśitamśiṣṭaṃ śāstra eva spaṣṭamiti sakalaṃ samañjasamśrīrastu iti śrīmatsāyaṇamādhavīye sarvadarśanasaṃgrahe sakaladarśanaśirolaṃkāraratnaṃ śrīmacchāṃkaradarśanaṃ samāptam samāptoyaṃ sarvadarśanasaṃgrahaḥ
